Hoover Reports to Congress on Adjusting War Debt Plan 62

Believes War Debt is Closely Related to Disarmament

Does Not Approve of Cancellation, Concessions Must Be Conditional

Advocates Forming a Committee for International Negotiations

National News Agency, Washington, 19th – U.S. President Hoover today delivered a special report to Congress on the war debt issue. His tone was extremely resolute, stating that he would swiftly proceed with negotiations to restructure the war debt, regardless of whether Congress approves. He also indirectly declared to the debtor nations in an even more firm tone that the United States should respect the requests for renegotiation from countries that maintain their debt obligations. However, for countries in arrears, negotiations will not begin until after the overdue payments due on December 15th have been made. The President’s report was read to both houses of Congress after the stock market closed to prevent any impact on the market. Its content is essentially a concise plan for a rapid adjustment of war debts, clearly indicating that the current payment schedule should be revised. However, it also clearly states that war debts cannot be canceled, and any concessions must be compensated for in other ways. The wording throughout implies that discussions will only be held with certain countries, not with those in arrears. In addition, he will propose to Congress the appointment of a bipartisan U.S. delegation to attend the World Disarmament Conference and authorize them to negotiate on the war debt issue. The selection of the delegates will require the consent of President-elect Roosevelt before a final decision is made. He stated that the situation is so urgent that we must cooperate nationally for the welfare of the American people and to overcome the forces that threaten the foundation of our culture. According to reports, Hoover’s words refer to the arrears in war debt payments and the failure of various countries to disarm. The report consistently treats war debts and disarmament as a single issue. He continued by stating that it is necessary to establish a suitable mechanism. Ordinary diplomatic channels and facilities are no longer adequate. Only by sending extremely qualified representatives to sit around a table can we expect the best negotiations. These representatives should be selected immediately to prepare for the World Economic Conference and exchange views on war debts with certain countries, as well as advise the government on the course of action to be taken with respect to other countries. (The report likely refers to countries in arrears when mentioning "other countries.") The President also stated that there would be significant benefits to coordinating these issues with the Disarmament Conference and emphasized that the issue of disarmament is the most important aspect of this problem, even more important than the arrears in payments due in December. He also cited statistics comparing European military spending with the amount paid on war debts, stating that, except for one country, the amount needed to repay debts is less than a quarter of their military expenditures. This also reveals where Hoover places the emphasis on the war debt issue. The report also stated that this plan is designed to prevent war debt negotiations from being affected by changes in government and to avoid delays in progress. The report indicates that this plan requires Congressional approval, but the President also stated that he believes the matter is extremely urgent and cannot be delayed any longer, and that he will initiate action himself, regardless of Congress’s actions.

Roosevelt's Opinion 63

Negotiations Should Proceed Through Ordinary Diplomatic Channels

National News Agency, Washington, 19th – The U.S. government is currently awaiting the reaction in Congress to the President’s war debt report. According to reports, President-elect Roosevelt prefers to conduct negotiations with debtor nations through ordinary diplomatic channels. He still believes that diplomats are well-suited to handle all the necessary negotiations, especially in the initial stages. He believes that the initial task is to investigate what European countries are currently capable of doing and to explore what methods they are willing to propose and accept. Therefore, he does not support the formation of a special committee to handle these negotiations.

Borah Expresses Support 64

Reuters, Washington, 19th – Senator Borah, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, issued a statement supporting President Hoover’s message to Congress. Borah also advocated for convening a world conference as soon as possible to address disarmament, currency, and war debt issues.

British Newspapers Unanimously Welcome 65

Reuters, London, 20th – London newspapers have widely published editorials welcoming President Hoover’s message to Congress on the war debt issue. Conservative, Labour, and Liberal parties share the same excitement. The Daily Telegraph (Conservative) stated that President Hoover’s message is welcomed in Britain because Britain has paid what it owes and hopes to reconsider the war debt issue on the best terms possible. The Daily Herald (Labour) stated that Britain can at least begin discussions with a genuine hope of achieving results, as the foundation has been laid. The Westminster Gazette (Liberal) stated that President Hoover’s declaration, regardless of any criticism it may receive in the United States, is truly courageous and deserves our gratitude and even our admiration.

Opportunities for U.S.-Soviet Rapprochement Further Advanced 66

Economic Reasons Transform into Political Reasons

Objective is to Counter Japanese Advances in Mainland Policy

Slogan: "The Enemy of My Enemy is My Friend"

New York – News of Sino-Soviet rapprochement has greatly excited American political circles and those concerned about the situation in the Far East. Opportunities for the United States to recognize the Soviet Union have therefore advanced further. It is anticipated that pro-recognition sentiment will peak with the inauguration of President Roosevelt. There has been a major shift in the Senate Foreign Relations Committee's attitude towards this issue, with nine members now in favor of recognition, five opposed, and seven undecided. President Roosevelt has publicly pledged to study this issue with an open mind, meaning he will favor recognition if it is in the best interests of the United States. Senator Borah, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, has submitted a resolution on the recognition of the Soviet Union to the committee, but stated that he will not press for a vote on the resolution until Roosevelt's attitude is more firmly expressed. However, President Hoover remains opposed to recognition and is likely to veto or block any pro-recognition proposals. In addition, patriotic groups and large commodity industries such as coal and lumber, fearing competition from Russian goods, are also vigorously opposing recognition. According to impartial observers, the first step on this issue will likely be to establish a committee to investigate trade relations with Russia and study U.S. demands towards Russia, such as the confiscation of property and denial of loans. Supporters of recognition have primarily based their arguments on the development of commerce, but now a political dimension related to the Far Eastern situation has been added, transforming the arguments. There is now a movement to quickly recognize and assist the Soviet Union to counter Japanese advances in mainland policy. These people believe that America's potential enemies are Japan across the Pacific and Europe across the Atlantic, so they advocate for the recognition of the Soviet Union with the slogan "The enemy of my enemy is my friend." These people believe that there are minimal conflicts of interest between the Soviet Union and the United States geographically, militarily, or commercially. Once the war debt issue among European and American countries is resolved, the United States will shift its attention to the Far East. However, the restoration of U.S.-Soviet relations will depend on various investigations after the new president takes office, and it is too early to say anything concrete at this time. (World News Agency)

Key Figures in the U.S. Democratic Party Discuss Far East Policy 67

Wilson's Right-Hand Man

Explains the Stimson Doctrine

New York – Colonel House, former President Wilson’s “right-hand man,” published an essay on several foreign policy issues facing the incoming Roosevelt administration in the latest issue of "Foreign Affairs Quarterly." His perspective as a Democrat on the foreign policy of a Democratic government has attracted the attention of readers. The essay states, "One of the most pressing issues in recent months has been the situation in the Far East. The United States has a dual interest in the Manchurian dispute. The first is to uphold the effectiveness of treaties, because upholding the effectiveness of treaties is part of the overall issue of maintaining international peace. The second is to uphold the traditional U.S. Open Door policy. Regarding this second point, our government's policy should be based on changes in the world and the Far Eastern situation, and should be open to negotiation. Secretary of State Stimson's doctrine, announced last year, focuses on two paths: either a return to the previous status quo through the voluntary actions of the two directly involved parties in the Manchurian dispute, or a resolution of outstanding issues through direct negotiations without further bloodshed." (World News Agency)

British-Persian Oil Dispute 68

Behind the Scenes, There is Activity by American Capitalists

Attempting to Oust Britain's Monopoly on Persian Trade

Italy Also Unwilling to Relinquish Rights

(League of Nations Decides to Postpone Discussion)

Reuters, Geneva, 19th – The League of Nations Council has now received a letter from the Persian delegation, in which they stated the threatening attitude of the British government towards Persia. The letter declared that the Persian government is willing to submit the matter to the Council, but requested a slight delay in the meeting so that the Persian representatives could return to Tehran to bring necessary documents to Geneva. It was also stated that the Persian government does not want to adopt any plans detrimental to the Anglo-Persian Oil Company before the Council makes a decision, so the matter is not urgent. The Council has now decided to postpone the discussion of this dispute until the next regular session in January. The Acting Chairman of the League of Nations Council, Mr. Loster, has now telegraphed to both the British and Persian governments, asking them not to take any actions that could aggravate the situation or expand the dispute while the Council is studying the matter, and declared that the Council has postponed the issue until the next regular session for further discussion.

Havas, London, 19th – British First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell today denied in the House of Commons the claim that the British government had sent warships to Persian territorial waters to protect British interests due to the dispute with Persia.

London – This British-Persian oil dispute is a major international capital war with complex underlying issues. On the Persian side, it is because the company did not comply with the contract to pay 16% of its profits to the Persian government, hence the strong stance. On the British side, it is believed that the original contract did not contain a clause on the abolition of concessions, and that the Persian government's decision to abolish the concessions is completely illegal. The damages suffered by the Anglo-Persian Oil Company are the responsibility of the Persian government. In addition, the cause of this dispute is actually the behind-the-scenes activities of American capitalists. American capital groups such as Morgan & Company, Goodyear Tire & Rubber Company, and General Motors Corporation have successively sent representatives to Persia to negotiate with the Persian government, seeking to overthrow Britain's monopoly on Persian trade. If American capitalists can obtain this exclusive right, they will organize a U.S.-Persian company with a capital of $2 million, and in addition to taking over all of Persia's imports and exports, they will also establish various factories and develop Persia's domestic industries. In addition, the Italian government has also issued a strong ultimatum to the Persian government, notifying them to suspend all negotiations until the Italian delegation arrives in Persia. The fact that the Persian government secretly sent a military mission to the United States three weeks ago to purchase several million dollars worth of military supplies has also recently been revealed. Therefore, this British-Persian dispute is the beginning of a major international capital war, and should not be taken lightly. (World News Agency)

They discussed several issues related to Russian-German relations. Judging from the discussions today, the two sides seem to be quite close in their views on the points discussed.

British House of Commons Surrounded by Unemployed 70

Reuters, London, 19th – Tonight, Prime Minister MacDonald was giving a radio broadcast appealing to the nation to find a livelihood for the unemployed. The House of Commons was debating a supplementary budget of £19 million to fund unemployment relief when a large group of unemployed people marched to the House of Commons, urging prompt relief for the unemployed and their families. Led by former Communist MP Saklatvala, representatives entered the House of Commons, attempting to meet with the Parliamentary Secretary to the Ministry of Labour. They were told to submit a written request, so Saklatvala and the representatives quietly withdrew, but the demonstrators still surrounded the House of Commons. They were later dispersed by the police without incident. When voting on the budget, Labour MPs proposed a formal amendment opposing the government's unemployment policies, which was defeated by a vote of 216 to 31.

New French Cabinet Holds First Meeting 71

Havas, Paris, 19th – The new cabinet held its first meeting today. Prime Minister Pongou gave an opening speech, saying, "From the organization of this cabinet, it can be seen that we have sincerity in our approach to governance and in continuing the previous work. Our reason for doing so is not only to honor Herriot's achievements, but also because our country's politics must continue the previous course. We are pursuing a policy of peace and building peace, a policy of democracy and building democracy, and a policy of revitalizing finance. Our appointment of Cheron as Minister of Finance demonstrates the government's desire to be sincere with the people. If the people can truly understand the real situation of the finances, they will certainly support the various necessary measures we take."

Reuters, Paris, 19th – The new French cabinet formed by Pongou was welcomed by the stock exchange here. Government bonds all rose in price today. Pongou convened his first cabinet meeting today to discuss administrative policies, which will be read in parliament on Thursday. The new government will announce the continuation of Herriot's policies, except for war debts. Herriot advocated paying the installment due this month on the condition that the United States was willing to reconsider the entire war debt issue. However, the new government insists that it will not pay the debt without a new solution. The new government must now propose a method of approving expenditures on a monthly basis to raise funds to get through the end of the year. Some believe that the Pongou government can only last until the New Year.

Silver Screen Star Earns Owner Six Million

Reuters, Hollywood, 19th – Tony, the famous horse who served on the silver screen with his owner Thomas Mix for twenty years, retired today. He is now twenty-three years old. Mix purchased him for nine U.S. dollars as a sick horse in 1909. He then personally fed him milk and oats, and after his strength was restored, he reappeared on the screen. He first appeared in a Selig Polyscope Company film in 1912. Since then, he has traveled through Europe and the Americas with his owner. There is almost no moviegoer who does not know his name, and he has helped Mix earn six million dollars. He recently injured his thigh while working on a film, and is now retiring. He will live in the most luxurious stable built by Mix.

Over One Hundred People Arrested in Connection

A Glimpse of Japanese Right-Wing Groups 74

Japan has been affected by the global economic panic, although not severely. However, domestic changes are very drastic. The Communist Party, after severe crackdowns, seems to have subsided on the surface. Many leading figures are in prison, and the general labor movement has entered a clandestine state due to market decline. Right-wing groups originally intended to oppose left-leaning ideologies and resist communism. Now that the left wing is engaging in secret activities and the social situation and the lives of the general public are deteriorating, even those who labor all day cannot achieve warmth and sustenance. Therefore, patriotic groups originally aimed at dealing with advanced ideas, except for refraining from infringing upon the Emperor and expressing respect for the powerful military, express active dissatisfaction with the current political parliamentary system and harbor particularly deep resentment towards financial capitalists. This is indeed an inevitable natural trend in Japanese society. However, it greatly deviates from the original intention of Japanese militarists to utilize right-wing ideology and the deep-seated intentions of political figures to cultivate patriotic thought. The most obvious and powerful proof of this is the assassination of Prime Minister Hamaguchi Osachi of the Minseitō cabinet. Amidst the fierce fighting in Shanghai, Inoue Junnosuke, a financial expert from the Minseitō, and Takuma Dan, a loyal servant of the Mitsui conglomerate, were assassinated one after another. On May 15th, at 5:30 PM, Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was shot and killed by active-duty military officers at his official residence. From then on, right-wing groups became even more rampant. If Prime Minister Saitō Makoto did not have the support of the navy, he would probably have followed in Inukai's footsteps. Since his inauguration (cabinet formed on May 28th), which was just over six months ago, there have been as many as four discovered assassination plots. Behind these violent acts, right-wing groups provide the underlying strength, while the instigators are said to have a separate "General Staff Headquarters."

In the navy, Marshal Tōgō Heihachirō leads everything. Next, Yamamoto Gonnohyōe, Saitō Makoto, Okada Keisuke, and others support and maintain its consistent system. However, in the army, after Yamagata Aritomo, there was only Tanaka Giichi. After Tanaka's death, Utsunomiya Katsusaburō should have been the successor based on seniority and prestige. However, although Utsunomiya had deep qualifications, his knowledge was relatively poor, and his skills were weak, so he could not lead the entire army. The army is divided into three factions. The former Minister of the Army, General Minami Jiro, General Kanaya Hanzō, and General Suzuki Sōroku, along with Lieutenant Generals such as Abe Nobuyuki (current commander of the Taiwan Army), Terauchi Hisaichi (commander of the 4th Division stationed in Osaka), Sugiyama Gen (commander of the 12th Division stationed in Kurume, Kyushu, one of the five special large divisions of the Japanese army), and Hayashi Senjūrō (leader of the retired lieutenant generals), are the mainstays of the Utsunomiya faction. Qin Zhenji (Lieutenant General, commander of the Kempeitai), Koiso Kuniaki (Lieutenant General, Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army stationed in Manchuria), and Kageyama Yoshitsugu (Lieutenant General), are the leading generals of the current Vice Chief of Staff, Mazaki Jinzaburō's faction. Although the Araki (Sadao) faction seems to encompass Mazaki on the surface, those who support Araki include General Mutō Nobuyoshi (current commander of the Kwantung Army). Mid-level officers include Major General Nagata Tetsuzan, Major General Itagaki Seishirō, Colonel Ishiwara Kanji, and Lieutenant Colonel Hashimoto Kingoro. These young officers all want to actively expand their military operations against China to exaggerate their achievements. Therefore, they mobilize veterans and incite the organization of right-wing groups to raise public morale, not knowing that the result is only to disrupt Japanese society and lead it into an incurable state. Japanese right-wing groups can be roughly divided into three major factions. The first category is purely nationalists. The second category is nationalists with some elements of modern thought. The third category is the right-wing of socialism, who approve of militarism and aggression, but attach conditions for the liberation of toiling workers and peasants. These three are described below.

The first category originated from the Gen'yōsha founded by Toyama Mitsuru. Its formation coincided with the Meiji Restoration. Initially, it was an organization for cultivating learning and training the body and mind. Later, it transformed into a Rōnin association specializing in invading China. In addition to Toyama Mitsuru, the giant of the nationalist faction, his colleague Uchida Ryōhei was a strong general of the society. Uchida was the center in establishing the Kokuryūkai. Although it also plagiarized some social policy proposals, established simple cafeterias, and ran workers' dormitories, it strongly advocated the mixture of Eastern and Western cultures, promoted Eastern culture, and severely criticized the bias of the rule of law. Therefore, it advocated developing the mysteries of Emperor worship, reforming the current system, resolving labor-management issues, revitalizing the martial spirit, and strengthening national defense agencies. Thus, Shiba Shirō had the Daitamin Club, Mori Kenji had the Taisho Sekishin Group, and Ishii Saburō, Ogawa Heikichi, and Lieutenant General Tachibana Koichirō also founded the Kōdōgikai, etc. Although the names are different, the content is the same. The Jūō Club was once rampant in the Waseda University district, and its struggles against left-wing scholars such as Nosaka Sanzō, Ōyama Ikuo, and Chō Kotsunan were particularly fierce. The first task of the Japan Great Nationalist Society, the Kantō Nationalist Society, the Yamato People's Labor Association, the New Japan Association, and the Anti-Reddening Group, etc., is to prevent the spread of left-leaning ideologies, to uphold the imperial family as the center, to overthrow Marxism, and to establish national authority. The Manchuria-Mongolia Group, the Shūsūikai, the Daitōsha, and the Great Japan Justice Group, although claiming to be anti-communist, place more emphasis on the invasion of the Northeast. The Tenkōkai and the Independent Youth Society, directly subordinate to the Rōnin Association and the Kokuryūkai, have transformed from external struggles to internal conspiracies, secretly importing military supplies and planning assassinations. As for the Great Japan Production Party, it is just a smokescreen, while the Kaiseikai and the Meirin Society, two military social groups, are actually the instigators behind the aforementioned groups. However, these soldiers mostly belong to the old school and have very high positions, and are far removed from the general public.

The second category is radical nationalist groups. The first organization established was the "Rōzōkai," formed by Ōi Kentarō, Ōkawa Shūmei, Mitsukawa Kametarō, Nakano Seigō, Takabatake Motoyuki, Shimanaka Yūzō, etc. Among them were nationalists, socialists, liberals, soldiers, and old parties. After Iwata of the Daikakai, Shimizu of the Daikōsha, and Tatsukawa and Ōkawa of the Shiranami-kai discussed, they established the Yūzonsha, using the national spirit as a creative revolution to build a revolutionary empire. Ōkawa Shūmei's Kōchisha, meaning "following heaven and earth," followed the guidelines of the Yūzonsha, which were to strongly oppose Japan's current complacency and to deeply resent contemporary zaibatsu. Therefore, it advocated actively invading Manchuria, but the spoils of invasion should be given to the Emperor, who would then bestow them upon his subjects. After the September 18th Incident, the society was unusually active in the Northeast. Due to conflicts with the military's policy of linking financial capitalists, it rejected the development of Japanese financial capital in the Northeast. As a result, Ōkawa was arrested in Dalian, and the activities of the Kōchisha were also hit. The Daikakai of Iwata Fumio, the Daikōkai of Shimizu Kōnosuke, the Shiranami-kai of Tatsukawa Shizuo, and the Tōkai Alliance of Ōsugi Seishi all arose after the dissolution of the Yūzonsha. Although their outlines and details are different, their essence is largely similar. The spirit of the Tōkō League, the Isshinkai, the All Japan Yōkokudōshikai, the Daihōsha, the Shirinsō, the Kokumin Sensensha, and the Jinbukai are inconsistent and their substance differs, but their general consciousness is the same as that of the Kōchisha. Ōkawa even served as the chairman of the Jinbukai. This faction has direct connections with the Kozakukai, the Sakurakai, and the Yōyōkai, which are social groups for middle and lower-ranking military officers. Therefore, military giants also interact with them, and Heisaka Kiichi of the Kokuhonsha and Lieutenant General Kikuchi Takeo also belong to this category.

The third category, the National Socialist Party, is the radical faction among Japanese right-wing parties. Its leading figures also came from the Social Democratic Party, such as Akamatsu Katsumarō, who was an actual labor activist of the faction, and Kondō Eizō and Hayashi Aokio, who were theorists of the faction. Hirano Rikizō led peasant organizations. Its theoretical magazine is "National Socialism." Nagano Akira is an actual guide in the rural movement, and Son Kwon-seong engages in theoretical struggles. Although its formation time is short and its mass power is weak, it is more active among right-wing groups.

The above is a brief description of the situation of Japanese right-wing groups, which is inevitably simplified, but it is largely complete. From this, one can also see the complexity within its right-wing groups. If the military does not meddle in it, its internal struggles will outweigh its external aggression. (Dispatch from Tokyo, December 14)

Inspection Record of Suppressing Communists and Recovering Various Areas (III) 75

Situation in the Jingzhou-Shashi Area

After the reporter accompanied the inspection group to inspect Yuekou Port on the Xiang River, at 9:00 AM on the tenth, they took a car westward from Yuekou to inspect the Jingzhou-Shashi area. At 11:00 AM, they arrived at Zhangjia Port, which is 45 li from Yuekou and located on the north bank of the Xiang River. It is an important route from Yuekou to Jiangling and is crucial in suppressing the communists. After the communists occupied Honghu, they advanced and occupied this area as a stronghold on the north bank of the Xiang River, invading Tianmen to the east, attacking Jingmen to the north, and attacking Jiangling to the west. From 1927, bandits frequently appeared here, demolishing civilian houses and building pontoon bridges on the Xiang River to connect with the bandit areas on the south bank of the Xiang River. The National Army repeatedly attacked and suppressed them, gaining and losing it at times. The communists occupied this place for a total of two years, causing extremely heavy losses. The residents' property was looted, and the houses were almost completely burned down. It was not until June or July of this year that it was completely recovered. Now, the people's livelihood is declining to the extreme. The residents have no way to make a living, and they dismantle and sell the bricks, tiles, and wood of all the remaining broken houses to exchange for grains to prolong their lives. Some even eat grass roots and tree bark every day. The miserable situation is unbearable to witness. Traveling west from Zhangjia Port, they arrived at Shayang at around 12:00 PM. This place is located in the middle reaches of the Xiang River, connecting Jiangling and Shashi to the west, Qianjiang and Honghu to the south, Tianmen to the east, and Zhongxiang to the north. It has always been a commercial center. In July of last year, the New Third Brigade suffered a defeat here and was occupied by the communists, who looted everything. It was not until October of last year that it was recovered by Zhang Zhenhan's 41st Division. Now, commerce is declining, finance is in a panic, and the general merchants and people are in extreme distress. The rural fields are barren, and the scene is even more desolate. The local militia in the city is well-organized, armed with broadswords. There are only a few primary schools for education, and there are not many students. According to Division Commander Zhang Zhenhan, the communists in Hubei were not paid attention to at first, which led to their spread. The stationed troops were busy fighting and were frequently transferred, so they could not concentrate on suppressing the bandits. After 1930, the Tenth Army returned from Henan Pass, but it only suppressed them locally. At that time, the troops stationed in Zoujing were weak, and they were fighting in the east and fleeing in the west, without a whole plan. After Commander Jiang (Jieshi) took office in Wuhan, he transferred a large army to block and suppress them in separate routes. After fighting for several months, he has achieved today's results. The reasons for the spread of the communists are partly due to the decline of the people's livelihood and partly due to the failure of the army to concentrate on suppressing them. The communists originally had only a few hundred guns, but they gradually increased after robbing the guns of the police and security teams in the various counties and towns. Now, although there are militia organizations for suppressing communists in various cities, towns, and villages, they are not enough to prevent bandits unless they are militarized and disciplined. The communists are organized tightly, and all soviets and troops are commanded by the Communist Party. The Party has supreme authority. In their battles, they concentrate all their strength on the front line and threaten the people to organize red guards and guerrillas to create momentum. They train the peasants very strictly, requiring them to hold meetings once a day and hold a large parade once a week, so that the general peasants have a group organization. As for the communists' methods of deceiving the people, they are also extremely clever, advocating resisting rent and taxes, overthrowing rich peasants, killing intellectuals, and improving the lives of workers and peasants. The general ignorant people were deceived at first, but now they have realized their deceit and seen through their treachery. At 6:00 PM on the tenth, they crossed the Yangtze River and arrived at Shashi via Jiangling. Today, they actually inspected Jiangling and Shashi. Jiangling is an ancient important town with many relics of Guan Yu, but they have mostly been submerged. In recent years, the city has been plagued by soldiers and bandits, and is dilapidated and desolate, unlike its former prosperity. The jurisdiction area is 700 li in circumference, and one-third of the county has been ravaged by the communists. The southern villages have suffered quite severely. According to a certain gentleman in the local area, Jiangling is harmed by soldiers and bandits more than by the Red Party. In the past, the village chiefs colluded with bandits, running rampant in the villages, and the official government could do nothing. The people had nowhere to appeal. In addition, Cui Erdan's troops were stationed in the Jingmen area, and the local bullies relied on them as a shield to collude with each other, making the people's lives unbearable. All of these things created opportunities for the communists. Now, the village teams are still the same as before, and the authorities are currently trying to rectify them, intending to confiscate the guns of all the teams and reorganize them to eliminate harm to the people. The political aspects have always been quite dark, and the authorities have recently been rectifying them. As for education, on the surface, many schools have been established, but in reality, few students enroll. In the past, educational funding was lacking, and the school authorities issued salary arrears vouchers indiscriminately. Those who held the vouchers colluded with the stationed troops to extort money from the county government. The county government, threatened by their power, had to pay according to the list, which led to many abuses. This spring, a certain army built an airport, demanding huge sums of money and setting a deadline for completion. The requisitions were sent out in all directions, urgent as a fire. The people's hardship was half caused by the poor discipline of the stationed troops. Now, Jingzhou and Shashi have been taken over by Xu Yuanquan's Tenth Army, and the military authorities are planning to find ways to relieve the people's difficulties and move towards a path of improvement. Although the communists in the Jingzhou-Shashi area have been cleared on the surface, there are still many who are lurking in the dark and plotting to take advantage of opportunities. In order to clear the bandits, the authorities are conducting a household registration survey and implementing the Baojia system. Shashi was originally a large port in the upper Yangtze River, and commerce was extremely prosperous in the past. In recent years, due to the influence of military affairs and the ravages of the communists, the rural villages in the four directions have gone bankrupt, and commerce has been severely hit. The general merchants are unable to maintain their businesses. In short, the area from Jingzhou and Shashi to the east of Hougang has been directly destroyed by the communists. Although the area west of Hougang has not been directly ravaged by the communists, the indirect impact is extremely great. It will not be possible to recover in a day or two. (Dispatch from Shashi, December 11)

Recent Situation in the Sichuan War 76

Chongqing Air News: The main bodies of the Sichuan War are Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui. Others, such as Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, Liu Cunhou, Li Jiayu, and Luo Zezhou, are just guests, only taking advantage of the mutual infighting between the two Lius to gain benefits. There was originally no inevitable momentum for war, but Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui were fighting to the death due to issues of survival. After the wave of cooperation from five divisions in Chengdu, the Sichuan War went from being dormant to active again. Liu Xiang amassed his troops and attacked Liu Wenhui fiercely, hoping to wipe out the 24th Army in one fell swoop. Seeing the situation was not good, Liu Wenhui automatically abandoned Chengdu and used all his strength to deal with the 21st Army. Therefore, there have been unprecedented fierce battles in the areas of Jiading, Renshou, and Jingyan recently, with an intensity never seen before. After Liu Wenhui withdrew from Chengdu, he convened a meeting of all the army generals in Meishan, unanimously deciding to bet on their final fate with the 21st Army. Xia Zhongshi was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the first route, commanding eight brigades including Yu Zhongying, Zhang Zhifang, Li Yushu, Gao Yucong, Peng Chengfu, Chen Xinmin, Liu Wencai, and Chen Mingqian, concentrated in Jiading. Leng Yindong was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the second route, leading five brigades including Zhao Peishan, Wang Yuanliang, Cheng Zimin, and Deng He, concentrated in Jingyan. Zhang Qingping was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the third route, leading six brigades including Xu Tingxiu, Wang Zhiren, Huang Xixuan, and Shi Zezhou, concentrated in the area between Renshou. Liu Wenhui personally led most of his troops, about eight brigades, concentrated in areas such as Meishan, Pengshan, and Jiajiang. On the sixteenth, the 24th Army began a general offensive, sending out three routes to attack the 21st Army fiercely. The 21st Army was caught off guard and suffered a major defeat, with all routes retreating below Xufu, almost to Luzhou. Liu Xiang was shocked to hear the report in Longchang and immediately moved to Zizhong, sending Commander-in-Chief Tang Shizun of the first route to lead four brigades to attack Jingyan fiercely. Wang Zhiyi of the second route led five brigades including Wang Zejun to attack Renshou fiercely. Fan Shaozeng of the third route led five brigades including Zhou Shaoxuan, Fan Nanxuan, and Meng Haoran to attack Jiading. Pan Wenhua led four brigades including Guo Xun and Fan Ziying to support the rear and mobilized ten aircraft and all artillery and machine guns to assist in the fierce counterattack against the 24th Army. On the seventeenth, Tang Shizun, Fan Shaozeng, Pan Wenhua, and Wang Zunxu's four divisions made contact with the 24th Army's Xia Zhongshi, Zhang Qingping, Leng Yindong, etc., and a great war broke out. The soldiers on the front line abandoned their rifles and used submachine guns, machine guns, fast-firing guns, and grenades to engage in fierce battles. Both sides also used daredevil teams in hand-to-hand combat. After a day of fierce fighting, the 24th Army suffered more than 16,000 deaths, Brigadier Li Yushu was seriously injured, Cheng Zimin was almost captured alive, and more than 20 regimental commanders were killed. The losses on the 21st Army side were even greater. Because the counterattack was fierce, the deaths exceeded 20,000. There are rumors that machine gun commander Liu Bingxun was killed in action. As a result, the 24th Army, unable to withstand the pressure of the opponent's air force, retreated to Jingyan, Jiading, Renshou and other places. Recently, Wang Zhiyi's troops of the 21st Army have advanced towards Renshou and have now occupied the Fajiachang and Zhangjiachang areas of Renshou. Pan Wenhua's troops have advanced to the Mataying area between Jingyan and Jiading. Tang Shizun's troops are stationed in the Qianfochang area of Jingyan. Fan Shaozeng is stationed in the Wutongqiao area of Jiading. There is also a regiment led by Liao Haitao attacking the Banqiaoxi area between Qingshen, Jiading, and Jingyan. Cheng Yinzhou's troops crossed Qianwei and advanced to Shibanxi. Liu Xiang himself has advanced to Rongxian, commanding everything, and set the date for a general attack on Jiading, Jingyan, and Renshou on the 20th. Currently, ammunition is being transported from the rear and the team is being supplemented. As for the troops stationed in Zizhong, Yang Sen, Li Qixiang, Luo Zezhou, etc., have also advanced forward. The three divisions have now occupied Guanyin Temple and Wengongchang in Renshou. However, the Chengdu side is silent and has entered a truce. However, there is now a shocking message, that the 21st Army has handed over the defense areas of the western Hubei counties to the Central Government, and Xu Yuanquan of the Central Army has sent troops to take over. Zhang Bangben, Luo Juntong, Tong Xigang, Wu Jintang, Yang Qinan and other troops returning to Sichuan are now scattered in the area of Dazhu, Linshui, Hechuan, Kaijiang, and Kaixian, all commanded by Wang Fangzhou. It is said that they are preventing Liu Cunhou's 20th Army and Yang Lin of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Army from taking advantage of the situation to attack the lower east and realize the conditions for the five-division alliance. In recent days, the Dazhu and Linshui areas have been very tense, with a storm brewing. If this matter is true, the future of the Sichuan situation will enter into a mixed war. (December 18)

Recent War Zone Map of Sichuan

Conclusion of the Jinan False Emperor Case 77

Li Lechuan Kowtows, Crying Injustice

Madam Song Wang Utters Nonsense

All Four Arrested Individuals Released

Jinan Correspondence: The case of the false emperor Li Lechuan and others, which once caused a sensation, was briefly interrogated by Han in the Provincial Government Hall yesterday morning and then ordered to be transported to the Public Security Bureau. At 8:00 PM tonight (the 18th), the prisoners were brought to the Provincial Government again, and Han personally interrogated them in his office. Those present included Shi Jingzhou, Chief of the Military Law Department, and Yang Jinbiao, Chief of the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau. Li Lechuan and Madam Song Wang kowtowed and refused to rise after entering the room. Han ordered them to sit, but they repeatedly said that commoners dared not sit. They finally sat after a long time. Han first said, "Don't be afraid. Perhaps you have your reasons. These are revolutionary times. Telling the truth doesn't mean anything." Li replied, "I truly dared not have any intention of becoming emperor." Han said, "I don't believe it either. One can't just become emperor so easily. I have two judgements about your case. 1) On the positive side, Buddhism has been prevalent in our country since ancient times, and believing in gods is not unusual. There are still evil cults like the Black Flag Society and Red Flag Society in Shandong. 2) On the negative side, perhaps you want to use a religious sect to gather many people. There have been many such cases throughout history, but promoting superstition is not good. You seem to be educated." Li replied, "My father died when I was seven, and I started studying at nine. In 1917 (民六), Shandong experienced a severe drought, and my mother sold over 100 mu of land..." Han said, "Even if you wanted to become emperor, you definitely couldn't do it in Jinan. It must be a religious sect. Who are your family members?" Li replied, "I have an elder cousin, Li Wenzao, who is acquainted with Zhang Weicun, a member of the Provincial Party Department, and Instructor Yan (of the private school). My family farms 80 to 90 mu of land and has no sons." Han said, "I see that you and the old lady (referring to Madam Song Wang) shouldn't be afraid. Tell the truth." Li said, "The newspapers have reported a great disaster." Han asked, "What are the oxen used for?" Li replied, "Various ceremonial items (i.e., semi-imperial paraphernalia) used in my cousin's (referring to Madam Song Wang) ancestral hall because her family had a prime minister during the Ming Dynasty and a Hanlin scholar during the Qing Dynasty." At this point, Han turned to ask the false empress Madam Song Wang, "How many sons do you have?" Madam Song Wang replied, "One. His father died when he was only one month and three days old. We have 48 mu of land. After my husband died, my relatives bullied me. I filed a lawsuit, and Magistrate Wu Baohe ruled in my favor. If my son reaches adulthood at fifteen, he will return to the Song family. If he doesn't reach adulthood at fifteen, he cannot return home. I had no choice but to take my child away." Han asked, "How do you make a living outside?" Madam Song Wang replied, "By treating illnesses." He asked, "How do you know how to treat illnesses?" She replied, "After coming out, I piously burned incense, offering 5,600 reams of paper and 3,600 sticks of incense. I held the incense while burning it, which damaged my hands and burned oil all over my body. Many women advised me not to burn anymore, so I didn't die, and they used a table to push me back. After the burns healed, I saw through the vanity of the world, didn't want to eat, didn't want property, and ate only one steamed bun every seven days, drinking plain water without salt, and then I started treating illnesses and fortune telling." He asked, "How do you tell fortunes?" She replied, "According to the Eight Trigrams and the Zodiac, I check when the sick child descended to earth, and then I tell them to find a doctor because my hands are burned and I can't use needles." He asked, "Why do you know how to treat illnesses and tell fortunes? Is it because gods or immortals are helping you? Tell the truth, it doesn't matter, I won't harm you." Madam Song Wang then kowtowed and said, "Only then do I dare to speak. After burning my hands, I no longer coveted the secular world. Although I wouldn't say I'm a god, I no longer speak ordinary words. I often tell my fellow believers that the world cannot last long and that Shandong will produce a real person to create a new world. Look at the Eastern Dipper, Western Dipper, and Southern Dipper, they have all succeeded. The Northern Dipper is the main palace. Only by believing in the Northern Dipper can you achieve peace, otherwise you will suffer a great calamity." Her followers grew daily. He asked, "How do you know the world will not last?" She replied, "I knew it after burning my hands. Wherever I go, I only drink plain water because the objects I made (referring to the semi-imperial paraphernalia) were repeatedly seized and interfered with by the authorities. The child of the Fu family was sick, and they asked me to see him. I taught them to do good deeds, ordering Elder Fu (referring to Fu Baoqi) to carry a grand feast. After going to Tai'an, they asked the palace to worship the gods. Because I came to Jinan to build a spirit tower, I settled down in Houyingfang Street, where I have lived for six years. This January, I went home, and in March, we came back together. My younger cousin (referring to Li Lechuan) came in June. When the Japanese devils were firing cannons (referring to the May 3rd Incident), I said Houyingfang Street would be fine, and Shandong would produce a real person to unify the world in peace. If a real person doesn't emerge, I am willing to be dismembered. I have never eaten salt, but after being arrested, my companions ate many beef buns, so I ate salt again. This is the truth. There is no religion. I am truly wronged." She then kowtowed again. He asked, "How do you know a new world will emerge and there will be a calamity?" She replied, "I calculated it according to yin and yang and the timing of heaven." He asked, "Who is the real person who can become emperor?" She replied, "If you approve my plea, you will definitely unify the world." Han laughed loudly at this and said, "I don't dare to become emperor, and how can you guarantee it?" Madam Song Wang suddenly said, "There has been no rain or snow this year." Han said, "If there is no rain or snow, it will be difficult to even eat, so how can you become emperor? Can you make it rain?" She replied, "With heavenly blessings, it can rain." Han said, "You have your reasons, but I don't dare to become emperor." Madam Song Wang replied, "I can guarantee that you will become emperor. If I can't, I am willing to be dismembered." Han then asked, "What is the use of the oxen you made?" Madam Song Wang kowtowed again and said, "The ox is a golden ox, a spring welcoming ox, waiting for the real person to be born. The sedan chair is stored in the Yixian Garden, and there is also a dragon bed, costing 3,600 yuan, made by a hundred princes, waiting for the real person to be born to offer tribute and seek rewards. Regarding the ox, there were negotiations a few days ago. Many carpenters who make oxen didn't know how, so I told them it was for the ancestral hall. After it was finished, I sought a pattern to give them. When making the ox, they put on clothes and fastened two flowers. However, the world is not awakened. The tower is a spirit tower, and I also made semi-imperial paraphernalia. I didn't want the flowers to be unfastened, and now I'm arrested again. Originally, I wanted to wait for the flowers to be fastened before sending them to you..." (As she said this, Madam Song Wang stood in front of Han, using a silk handkerchief in her hand, repeatedly making the shape of a flower, saying, "This is sunlight, this is moonlight, the Three Principles of the People, the blue sky and white sun.")

The day before yesterday, in the courtroom, you didn't kill me. When I returned, I said to my companions, "You are gracious, and you also gave us rations." I originally didn't eat, so I also bought a bowl of porridge to drink, and I bought side dishes for them to eat. Han, seeing that Madam Song Wang was babbling and seemed to have a mental illness, spoke kindly to her, saying, "Old lady, your hardships are not easy. Your husband died twenty years ago. I ask you, how much land do you have now?" Madam Song Wang replied, "I still have 60 mu." Han then turned to Li Lechuan and said, "You have studied and perhaps understand the reasoning. You can persuade her." Li said, "She is a bit confused. This time, we came to Jinan to build a tower. If the tower had been built, we would have left long ago." Han said, "Don't listen to the outside clamoring, but you should also be careful. These are revolutionary times, and parading imperial paraphernalia is too ostentatious." Madam Song Wang replied, "That's what my enemies say." Han said, "Even if you shout in the streets that you want to become emperor, I won't kill you, but you shouldn't act like this. If you are carelessly dealt with, you will be wronged. As chairman, I want to ensure the people's peace. You shouldn't shout and disturb people's hearts. I hope you don't act like this and go home to farm. And after returning home, persuade those who believe in religion in the Linyi area not to be superstitious anymore. As for you, old lady, how can you guarantee that I will become emperor? If you say you have magical powers, the gods cannot protect you. If you are shot, can the gods protect you? They definitely cannot protect you. If they could protect you, the Public Security Bureau wouldn't have been able to arrest you." At this point, the false Emperor Fu Baoqi and carpenter Zhi Huazuo were brought in. The two kowtowed incessantly. Han then asked Li Lechuan and Madam Song Wang, "I just advised you to go home and not to do such things again and to live peacefully. Do you believe what I say?" The four kowtowed together like pounding garlic and said, "We believe you, we dare not do it again." Han said, "If you cause trouble again, the government won't be able to ignore it. Alright, go home tomorrow." The four heard this and felt like they had escaped from death. They kowtowed endlessly. Han ordered them to be released that night and asked if they had travel expenses. When they said they didn't, he said he would give them some. They all said they had some. He then ordered the prisoners to be led out and released, and all the divine oxen, towers, clothes, and semi-imperial paraphernalia were left behind to be destroyed. This case was thus concluded. (Night of the 18th)

Songjiang

Request for Exemption from the Two-Yuan Grain Tax Increase 78

This year's winter grain tax, the Finance Department ordered the county to continue collecting an additional two yuan per stone of grain tax, as in previous years. The various agencies of the Financial Affairs Department, citing the low price of grain harming farmers and the inability of the people to pay, telegraphed the Provincial Government Finance Department to exempt them. Now, local gentry, such as Du Ruozhou, also requested exemption from the grain tax increase, citing the drastic drop in rice prices and seeking to alleviate the people's suffering, submitting separate petitions to the Ministry of Finance, the Provincial Government, and the Finance Department. The documents stated briefly: "Paying grain tax to the national treasury is the responsibility of the people, while the people's livelihood is the essence of the Party's state-building, which is what the government must do. Only by considering both can the country be rich and the people prosperous. The grain tax of five yuan has been the established system since the founding of the country. Two years ago, an additional two yuan per stone was levied for the Northern Expedition expenses, which was only a temporary expedient. Last year, following the previous example, the additional levy placed too heavy a burden on the people. We urge that it be exempted. We were graced with your instructions, stating that the additional two yuan grain tax for this year is to pay for the bandit suppression troops, and there is no way to offset it. It has been approved for one year. We see that you truly limit the alleviation of the people's livelihood. Although the price of rice was high last year, the people's burden was heavy, but they could barely manage to pay. This year, the price of rice has plummeted, and farmers' rental income is less than two-thirds of last year's. The first installment of the land price tax, along with the survey expenses, is already heavier than in previous years, and the second installment of the land price tax continues to levy an additional two yuan grain tax. Although national plans and people's livelihoods are difficult to balance, even if there is a shortage in the national plan, we can still consider making up the shortfall from other sources. As for the farmers, after the disasters of war, their savings are depleted, and it is already difficult to maintain their livelihoods. How can they have any remaining ability to pay the additional grain tax? Moreover, there was a clear order for the additional grain tax last year, how can it be extended again? We have a patriotic heart and the desire to turn stones into gold. Therefore, we request that the previous year's limited precedent be followed and that the continuation be exempted to alleviate the people's suffering."

Changshu

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire at Ma Si Bridge 82

Ma Si Bridge Town, located in the fifth district of this county, is located on the coast, and bandits can easily come and go. In the middle of last month, a kidnapping case occurred in the home of Dong Jieyuan in the town. Two young hostages were rescued from Nantong. On the day before yesterday (the 18th), another bandit alarm occurred in the town. About forty or fifty bandits, traveling on two fast boats, were detected by the local militia police, who immediately opened fire to suppress them. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle for an hour. The bandits eventually succumbed and fled. The situation is described as follows: At about 9:00 PM on the 18th of this month, several residents were returning home from a teahouse and vaguely saw two fast boats in the harbor, and there were shadows of people on the shore. Suspecting something was wrong, they crawled through the fields to observe their movements. Unexpectedly, more and more people were landing, so they ran to report to the Wangjiaqiao Militia Regiment and telegraphed the Fifth District Office to mobilize more than 30 regiment soldiers, armed with rifles and ammunition, and rushed to Ma Si Bridge. At that time, many bandits had already landed, each holding a rifle, about fifty or more people. As soon as the regiment soldiers arrived, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest, and the soldiers returned fire. The two sides exchanged fire for about 30 minutes. At that time, the county police team stationed in Si Yang also heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. The guns on both sides fired as densely as beads, and after about an hour, the bandits could not hold out and retreated. The police and regiment then chased to the riverside, but the bandit boats had already escaped.

They seized more than 30 bags of drug pills, manufacturing machines, and a total of more than 100 pieces of medicine, and a large bundle of printed Living Buddha old brand, double-opened as a record of the posting, and dozens of bags of pill boxes. The principal offender, Liu Jiapeng, was not inside, only fifteen employees, including Zheng Yusheng, were arrested together with twenty-two carts of evidence and sent to Zhenjiang via Boxian. Navigation Near Zhenjiang to Be Closed for Half a Day for Ten Days Starting Today 86

Inspecting the Fortress' Live Ammunition Shooting

Notice to Chinese and Foreign Shippers

The Ministry of Military Affairs is inspecting the various fortresses of the Yangtze River Fortress and firing live ammunition shells to test the projectile force range. A committee will be organized, prior to the meetings of the departments of Transportation, Foreign Affairs, Navy, each department, consulting on the locking of the channels during the inspection. This matter has been reported in this newspaper, and now the Committee has decided to first inspect the fortresses of Zhenjiang. The ban on navigation notice has arrived in Shanghai. Details are listed as follows.

Inspecting the Zhenjiang Fortress 87

The Yangtze River Fortress, now resolved by the committee, will first inspect four fortresses in Zhenjiang, specifically: 1) Xiangshan, 2) Jiaoshan, 3) Doutian Temple, 4) Tushan. When inspecting the four platforms, live ammunition shells will be fired. The inspections are divided into two routes: Xiangshan, Jiaoshan, and Doutian Temple as one route, and Tushan as the other route. From 3:00 AM today (the 21st) to 12:00 PM, the shooting time, will last until December 30th. Within ten days, the inspection of the four platforms will be completed.

Notification of the Navigation Restriction Range 88

Mr. Cleary, of the Zhenjiang Customs River Patrol, yesterday issued an urgent notice to shipping companies in Shanghai, saying that the Zhenjiang four fortresses are firing live ammunition for inspection, and the waterway is ordered to be closed within the firing range. The committee has decided to send four small vessels to anchor three kilometers outside the range of the shells, with red flags during the day and red lights at night, indicating the navigation ban. In the Xiangshan, Jiaoshan, and Doutian Temple route, the blocked area will be from Jiaoshan to Dantu Town. Two boats will be anchored at each location, with personnel stationed on the boats to monitor. In the Tushan Fortress route, the blocked area will be from Dagang Town to Sanjiangkou. One boat will be anchored at each location. All these restricted areas are prohibited from navigation.

Notice to Chinese and Foreign Warships and Vessels 89

The urgent notification has been sent by the Zhenjiang Customs to Shanghai, distributed to Chinese and foreign shipping companies, and forwarded to Yangtze River vessels. During this inspection period, from 3:00 AM to 12:00 PM every day, the vessel is not allowed to enter the above restricted areas. Vessels can still travel in the afternoon. If the red flag is not lowered, they cannot sail without permission. Foreign warships will be notified by the Navy Department, and civilian ships and barges will be issued notices by the civil affairs agencies, and the public will be notified to avoid misunderstanding and panic.

Continued Inspection of Other Fortresses 90

After the inspection of the four Zhenjiang fortresses, the committee will continue to inspect the Jiangyin Wolf Mountain and other platforms. It has been decided to go to Chengjiang to test-fire live ammunition shells again in early January. The navigation ban measures will be determined at that time and announced separately. It is reported that the inspection committee has gone from Beijing to Zhenjiang.

Record of Inspection of the New County Seat 91

Preserving the Ancient Bell Tower to Start Work Next Month

The Shanghai County Government will move the county seat on New Year's Day next year. Shanghai elders have launched a campaign to preserve the Mingxin Temple bell tower in Beiqiao, and the project is also scheduled to begin at the beginning of next year. The reporter of the China East News Agency inspected the new county seat yesterday and has considerable value in recording, as follows.

Photo of the front of the new Shanghai County Government (China East News Agency Photo)

The New County Seat is in Beiqiao Town 92

The municipal building is a road, planted with peach, willow, and plum blossoms. In front is the Zhuyehang, on the left is the new building of the County Party Department, and inside the gate, on the right is the Zhou Pan Room of the Public Security Section, on the left is the reception room and garage. In the middle is Shuiting Road, with lawns on both sides. The craftsmen are doing painting work, so the house doors are still locked and cannot be found everywhere. The building is only three floors. The upper floor is the conference room, the second floor is the county government and the construction bureau office, and the lower floor is the financial and education bureau office. The auditorium is behind, quite grand. Behind the building is a bungalow, the left is the office of the future Land Bureau, the right is the detention center, and in the middle is the dormitory for the chief police officer of the Public Security Section, classroom washroom, public cafeteria, and preliminary trial court. Outside the left side door, the Financial Bureau's money and grain counter will be built to facilitate the people's payment of grain and taxes. Outside the right side door, it is planned to set up a police entertainment troupe, allowing each police officer to arrange it at will, and the other part will be opened as a training ground. Outside the back door, a public toilet is being built, which will be completed at the same time as the new county seat.

Ancient Mingxin Temple Bell Tower 93

One of the ancient sites of Beiqiao, the temple has been expanded and destroyed, leaving only stone piers, west of the Shanghai-Min Road. The bell tower and tile tower are on the east side of the road. The tower has been deserted, and although the bell tower is dilapidated, it is still towering on the side of the road. Niu Yongjian, Wang Yiting, and others previously launched a campaign to preserve it, following the Tang sculpture of Jiaozhi. The county government has now formulated a plan to move the bell to the park and build a new building to store it. The bell weighs a thousand catties, and the four pillars of the building are also Phoebe zhennan wood, estimated to be worth more than 1,500 yuan. When moving the bell, the four pillars will also be moved to the new building, otherwise, it may not be able to bear the weight of the bell. The relocation project is scheduled to take place at the beginning of next year.

Japan's Foreign and China Trade for Eleven Months 95

Excess of Imports for Foreign Countries...Excess of Exports for China

The Japanese Commercial Counselor's Office in Shanghai received an official telegram from its home country yesterday, reporting that Japan's foreign trade for the eleven months of this year was worth a total of 2,508 million yen, of which exports accounted for 1,237 million yen, resulting in an excess of imports of 33 million yen. Compared with the foreign trade during the same period last year, the total amount increased by 14%, exports increased by 16%, and imports increased by 13%. Therefore, the amount of import excess can be reduced by 44% compared to the same period last year. However, if the import excess of overseas territories is included, the import excess for eleven months is still about 70 million yen.

As for trade with China, the total amount for eleven months was 198 million yen, of which exports accounted for 133 million yen, resulting in an excess of exports of 67 million yen (which in Chinese terms is an excess of imports). Compared with the export volume during the same period last year, exports to North China increased by 39%, exports to Central China decreased by 44%, exports to South China decreased by 92%, and exports to Hong Kong decreased by 56%. Compared with the import volume during the same period last year, imports from North China decreased by 25%, imports from Central China decreased by 41%, imports from South China decreased by 36%, and imports from Hong Kong decreased by 77%. Japan's trade with the Northeast three provinces was worth a total of 238 million yen, of which exports accounted for 126 million yen, resulting in an excess of exports of 13 million yen.

(Equal Protection for Chinese and Foreign People)

(External Correspondence Not Yet Received)

Since the Japanese side has repeatedly crossed boundaries to arrest naturalized Korean residents, naturalized Korean residents in Shanghai are extremely panic-stricken. Strike of All Messengers at Three Foreign Telegraph Offices Yesterday 97

City Party Headquarters Sends Personnel to Mediate

Still Unresolved as of Last Night

Over seventy messengers from the Great Northern, Great Eastern, and Pacific Telegraph Companies collectively went on strike due to prior demands for improved treatment, leading to a labor dispute. The dispute was temporarily resolved when the General Manager, Peng Sun, avoided the issue by going to Japan, and a temporary across-the-board wage increase of two dollars was given, pending further negotiations upon the General Manager's return to Shanghai. The messengers' union, the Third District Foreign Affairs Telegraph Workers' Union, noted that the General Manager had been back in Shanghai for some time but had not mentioned the matter. Consequently, on November 25th, they again sent representatives to present nine demands to the company. However, the management repeatedly procrastinated and provided no definite response. Unable to endure it any longer, the workers held a meeting the night before last and unanimously decided to strike. The strike went into effect at six o'clock yesterday morning. After the strike, all messengers left the office and gathered at a certain location, petitioning party and government agencies for assistance. The management immediately hired over a dozen Western children to deliver important telegrams for foreign businesses. For the remaining telegrams, customers were notified by telephone and asked to send someone to pick them up. Upon receiving the report, the City Party Headquarters dispatched Dai Yongchan to mediate, contacting both labor and management to discuss reconciliation methods. However, as of last night, there was still no news of work resumption.

Recent News on the Extraterritorial Road Construction Case 100

Hopes for Resolution by Next Spring

Information from the Japanese Consulate

Regarding the case of road construction by the Public Concession beyond its boundaries, it was heard yesterday that Japanese Consul General Ishii Taro had, on Saturday of the previous week, paid separate visits to the leaders of the Consular Body, Mr. 克银汉, British Consul General Mr. 利南, and Chairman of the Municipal Council Mr. 費信惇, for further substantive talks. The results of these talks have attracted considerable attention from Chinese and foreign residents in the city. A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency inquired at the Japanese Consulate about the details. A spokesperson admitted that Ishii had visited the British and American Consuls General and 費信惇 on Saturday but indicated that it was not solely to discuss the extraterritorial road construction case. It was because the commander of a Japanese naval squadron circumnavigating the world was scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 22nd, and the meeting was also to arrange a meeting with them. The spokesperson continued by saying that the Japanese side had, in principle, agreed to return the extraterritorial roads to China and was currently discussing the handover procedures to facilitate signing. He believed that there would be no further opportunity for consultation before Christmas this year but was confident that a resolution could be reached early next year. Although his remarks mentioned the issue of deputy police chiefs, the request was still being pursued, but he did not specify the trend. Furthermore, his attitude was not as resolute as before, suggesting that some understanding had been reached between the two sides.

Where is the Japanese Bushido Spirit?

Second Lieutenant Nishio Takes Own Life in Shame

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 20th: Like Major Kuken, Second Lieutenant Nishio, to live up to the spirit of Bushido, committed suicide. It has been a part of the sad history of the Shanghai Incident but has remained unpublished. The embargo on the story was lifted yesterday afternoon. The summary of the event is as follows: Nishio Jinroku, age 28, a reserve infantry second lieutenant from Kawamichi 1790, Daigo Village, Higashi Asai County, Shiga Prefecture, was appointed leader of a platoon in the 19th Regiment upon mobilization of the Kanazawa Ueda Division during the Shanghai Incident. He came to Shanghai to fight. Later, in a fierce battle at Jiangwan, he, like Major Kuken, was seriously wounded and taken prisoner by the Chinese army. After the war, he was returned to the Japanese army, but the second lieutenant deeply considered this the greatest shame to the spirit of Bushido. Overcome by a sense of self-reproach, he fell into extreme neurasthenia. After being sent back to his homeland, he refused visitors and acted cautiously. Suddenly, on the 10th of this month, taking advantage of a moment when his family was not watching, he sat properly in his room and bowed remotely to the Imperial Palace and the Ise Grand Shrine before calmly committing suicide with his family's treasured sword. Before committing suicide, on the 8th, he bid farewell to his mother, saying, "I will follow Major Kuken in committing suicide in the next day or two. I apologize in advance. My soul will permanently protect the country after death." His mother advised him to act as if he were already dead and devote himself to the country. On the 10th, he resolved to commit suicide.

Increase in Ship Fees Due to Low Water Level in the Yangtze River 104

Effective from the 26th

As winter approaches, the water level in the Yangtze River has been receding sharply in recent days. Heavy-laden riverboats can no longer navigate the section from Jiujiang to Hankou. Yesterday, six companies, including Taibao, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and China Merchants, agreed to increase shallow water fees. After public consultation, it was decided to uniformly increase the fees by 15% starting on the 26th. Announcements have been issued to inform all passengers.
