Record of Survey of the Yi Luo River Embankment Works 107

The National Government Flood Relief Committee Embankment Survey Group's special train departed from Yancheng on the 15th evening and arrived in Zhengzhou on the 16th, where they changed to a special train prepared by the Longhai Railway Bureau. They first went to Kaifeng, where the members of the Henan Provincial Government led them to the Yellow River to view the site proposed by the Henan Construction Department for using Yellow River irrigation water. That evening, they traveled west to Luo, and on the 17th morning, the train passed Gongxian, where leaders of various agencies and groups invited them to view the flooding of Gongxian city. At noon, they arrived in Luoyang to survey the Southern Pass Stone Embankment. At 2:00 PM, they crossed the Luo River to Longmen to survey the Yi River Embankment Works and view the Northern Dynasties stone carvings of Buddha statues. On the 18th, they went to Mengjin to survey the condition of the collapse of the Han River Light Wuling due to water erosion. In the evening, the special train departed from Luo and traveled east to Xuzhou, where it transferred to the Jinpu Railway to Bengbu Zhengyangguan Fengtai Wuhe and other places to survey the Huai River Embankment Works. Detailed information is recorded as follows:

Along the Longhai Railway 108

At 8:00 AM on the 16th, they arrived at Zhengzhou Railway Station. Administrative Inspector Meng Guangpeng and gentry Wei Manqing, among others, came to the station to welcome them. Zhang Jingyu, Director of the Henan Provincial Construction Department, and Du Fudong, Acting Chairman of the Provincial Relief Committee, also arrived in Zhengzhou from Kaifeng to welcome them. They were invited to breakfast at the Hua'an Hotel. During the meal, Inspector Meng delivered a welcome speech, followed by Wei Manqing's report on the progress of Henan Province in implementing urgent relief, work relief, and agricultural relief. Xi Mingjiu, Shi Dubei, and Li Mengping responded. Zhang Jingyu and Du Fudong also stood up to deliver speeches welcoming them to Bian and reporting on the disaster situation in southern Henan. At approximately 10:00 AM, they changed to the special train prepared by the Longhai Railway. Because Zhang Fang, the commander of the 20th Route Army in charge of handling the aftermath of the Special Zone in Southern Henan, needed to consult with Wen Lant亭, Li Zushen, and other gentlemen regarding relief efforts in the disaster area of Southern Henan before proceeding to Beijing, they first went to Kaifeng. They arrived at the station at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. Provincial government officials, with the exception of Zhang Jingyu, who traveled with them from Zhengzhou, Zhang Fang, Li Jingzhai, Acting Director of the Department of Finance Li Wenhao, and Secretary-General Fang Qidao, among others, came to the station to welcome them. They were invited to lunch at the Party, Government, and Military Joint Entertainment Society. After lunch, they traveled by automobile to the Yellow River to inspect the water diversion site. They then returned to the city to visit various antiquities from the Yin, Zhou, Tang, and Song dynasties in the museum, and toured the Iron Pagoda and Dragon Pavilion, among other places. The provincial government hosted a banquet in the evening, serving Kaifeng's special Yellow River carp. After the meal, they went to the All-Sector Welcome Meeting at the Yizhi Theater. Zhang Fang chaired the meeting and delivered a speech. Wen Lant亭, Li Zushen, Shi Dubei, and Lu Yiyu delivered speeches in succession, and a humanitarian film was shown. At 11:00 PM that evening, the special train traveled west, and at 7:00 AM on the 17th, they arrived in Gongxian. They climbed a mountain to remotely survey the flooded county seat. At 10:00 AM, they passed the White Horse Temple and stopped to visit. At 12:30 PM, they arrived in Luoyang, where leaders of various agencies came to the station to welcome them. After surveying the Southern Pass Stone Embankment on the West Pass, local residents welcomed them at the Southern Pass Crossing, with colorful awnings and high platforms. After speeches by Xi Mingjiu and Li Zushen, photographs were taken. They crossed the Luo River to the south to Longmen to survey the Yi River project and returned. That evening, the 11th District Administrative Inspector and various agencies and groups hosted a banquet at the West Station to welcome them.

Yi Luo Project 109

The Yi Luo Project under the 18th District Work Relief Bureau involved repairing 199 li of embankments, protecting over 200 villages and settlements, and over 6,300 qing of land, with an expenditure of over 237,000 yuan. An additional 116 li of canals were built under the urgent relief project, irrigating 848 qing of land, with an expenditure of 23,200 yuan. What was inspected on the 17th was the Six Embankments of the South Pass of Luoyang. They traveled by rickshaw from the station to the bank of the Luo River in front of the West Engineering Camp. When Wu Peifu was in Luoyang, he spent 300,000 yuan to build a Tianjin Bridge that spanned the Luo River. The project was quite solid, but the bridge openings were too small and the bridge deck too low, so it could not discharge water during floods. Therefore, within a year of completion, both ends were washed away by the flood, and only the middle section remains to this day. When the water rises, the flow is blocked in the middle, and the water surges sideways, causing considerable collapse on both banks. What was seen on the south bank was several zhang beyond the old bank, and the north bank was even worse. Therefore, the South Open Stone Embankment, starting near the Tianjin abandoned heap and extending to the Great King Temple, is a total of 2,208 meters long. Two rows of wooden stakes are driven into the embankment foot, and concrete and rammed earth are used to build a height of two meters. The outer slope is built with stone slabs and rammed earth. Three drainage dams, each 130 feet long, are built in the middle of the embankment, costing a total of 115,000 yuan, providing protection for Luoyang. Later, they traveled by automobile to Longmen Street to survey the Yiyang Balitang Embankment and tour the Buddha statues carved on the mountain walls on both sides of the Yique Longmen from the Northern Dynasties, numbering in the thousands, but mostly damaged.

Han Mausoleum River Dam 110

At 10:00 AM on the 18th, they traveled by automobile across the Northern Mang Mountain to Mengjin, passing the place where the Dragon Horse carried the diagram, and arrived at Tiexie Town, a distance of 60 li. They proceeded another li and paid their respects to the tomb of Emperor Guangwu of the Han Dynasty. They then went to the riverbank to observe the water situation. There are embankments on the south bank of the Yellow River starting from the Pinghan Railway Bridge. Above the Iron Bridge, the Northern Mang Mountain serves as a natural embankment. However, Mengjin County is located between the Yellow River and the north of the Northern Mang Mountain, and there are no high and thick embankments along the river to prevent flooding. A request has been made to Zhong　to specially build the Han Mausoleum Dam to protect the tomb of Emperor Guangwu. Several years ago, the dam bank was eight feet higher than the riverbank, and the water did not exceed the dam even during high water. Today, however, sediment has accumulated and submerged the dam, and the riverbed is level with the dam bank. The river channel is very small in the winter when the water is low, and the Han Mausoleum Tiexie is completely submerged in the water when the water rises in the spring and summer. Residents are requesting the construction of a stone dam fifteen li long, which would require an expenditure of 100,000 yuan. However, the river body is directly facing the Guangwu Mausoleum from the bend, and the water flow rushes straight down. After passing Tiexie East, the river returns to its original course a li or so away. It is feared that a single thin embankment will not be able to defend against it. At 3:30 PM, they returned to Luoyang from Tiexie. The car traveled in the Northern Mang Mountain, up and down steep slopes, encountering danger three times, but fortunately no disaster occurred. They finally arrived at the West Station at 5:30 PM. The special train traveled east at 7:00 PM and arrived in Xuzhou at noon on the 19th, where they changed to the Jinpu Railway to travel south. After arriving in Bengbu, they transferred to Zhengyangguan to survey the Fei River Embankment and the Wuhe Huai River Embankment. (Xinsheng News Agency)

Public Concession Implements New System of Weights and Measures 111

Municipal Government and Municipal Council Once Discussed Yesterday

The French Concession of this city had already negotiated and reached an agreement last winter regarding the new system of weights and measures, allowing the Municipal Government to send personnel to inspect at any time. However, in the Public Concession, although the Municipal Government had once discussed the matter, no formal solution has been decided. The Municipal Government believed that the failure to implement the new system in the Public Concession was unfair to the residents of the Chinese and French Concessions and would lead to many malpractices. It should be negotiated as soon as possible to resolve the issue. Therefore, at 2:00 PM yesterday, the Municipal Government invited the Public Concession Municipal Council to send personnel to discuss the matter at the Hua'an Building. The Municipal Government was represented by Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Head of the Second Section of the Social Affairs Bureau Wu Huanru, and Director of the Weights and Measures Inspection Office Zhou Zanming. The Municipal Council was represented by Mr. Qiwun and Mr. Wente. According to Secretary-General Yu's statement to the Central News Agency, the Municipal Council Chairman was unable to attend in person today (i.e., yesterday), so there was no result. However, Mr. Qiwun and Mr. Wente agreed to accept this intention, and the Municipal Government believed that since the new system has been implemented in the Chinese and French Concessions for a long time, it was inappropriate for the Public Concession to be the only one not implementing it. Therefore, the Municipal Government hoped that this matter could be completely resolved in the shortest possible time.

Tang Jiju Sends Telegram to Thank Donors 113

The troops of Tang Jiju, fighting fiercely in western Liaoning, have become increasingly strained since the withdrawal of Su Bingwen's army. Due to detailed circumstances, it has not been distributed. Our troops are not only continuing to fight, but also have a unit going to the Rehe border. Note that when Tang's troops attacked Shenyang, the Northeast Volunteer Army had remitted 10,000 yuan, which was transferred by the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in Beiping. Geng Jizhou Sends Telegram to Beg for Assistance 114

The Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Support Association received a telegram yesterday from Geng Jizhou, Commander-in-Chief of the Volunteer Army in western Liaoning, briefly requesting assistance. The original text is recorded below: "To the esteemed enemies: Since the Japanese invaders attacked, the entire nation has been united in hatred. Our army, grieving the loss of our homeland and hating the rampant Japanese, is filled with righteous indignation and vows to kill the enemy to bring glory to our nation and fulfill our national duty. Therefore, we have rallied our comrades and resolved to resist Japan. We have fought bloodily for many years, and the enemy's forces have been repeatedly defeated. However, there is no undefeated army in the world, and weapons have varying degrees of sharpness. When engaging in hand-to-hand combat, the miserable sounds are unbearable to hear, and the scenes of sacrifice are unbearable to witness. Driven by righteousness, how can we bear to silence the drums and cover the flag? Although our anger is suppressed, we must continue to exert ourselves in order to drive the thieves beyond our borders and restore our homeland. Enduring hardship and pain, we vow to deal with them to the end. We first raised the banner of righteousness in Qinmin, and then divided our troops with the Liaoning Army in western Liaoning. Wherever we go, the people welcome us, and our army has been able to successively capture Jin County, Jinxi, Beizhen, Yixian, Panshan, Taian, Xinmin, Zhangwu, Faku, Tieling, Kaiyuan, Kangping, Xingcheng, and Suizhong counties, all thanks to the assistance of the people. However, our troops are numerous, and expenses are also large. We lack both food to fill our bellies and weapons to kill the enemy. Although we have received support from patriotic and righteous people from all walks of life, it is like a drop in the bucket and does not help the situation. At this moment, the weather outside the Great Wall is unusually cold, and the anti-Japanese soldiers are still without adequate clothing. The miserable situation is self-evident. If assistance is not provided quickly, it will be difficult to sustain. According to reports from Yang Yijie, our army's representative who has returned to the unit, the gentlemen of your association are highly respected, possess sincere patriotism, and are particularly concerned about our army. We are deeply grateful for your kindness and friendship. Therefore, we are sending this special letter to you, respectfully requesting your assistance so that our soldiers can fulfill their original intentions. Then the country will be fortunate, and our army will be fortunate. We have presented our urgent words and await your orders. Respectfully, Geng Jizhou, Commander-in-Chief of the Volunteer Army in western Liaoning. To the esteemed Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Support Association."

The Liming Warship Launched Yesterday 117

In order to increase its naval power for bandit suppression, the Jiangxi Provincial Government entrusted the Shanghai Naval Shipyard to build two shallow-water gunboats this autumn. Yu Weifu, Deputy Director of the Shipbuilding Department of the Shipyard, went to Jiangxi in person to negotiate and sign the contract. After Yu returned to Shanghai, construction began immediately. Most of the project is now complete, and the ships have been named Liming and Fuxing. The Fuxing is nearly complete, and the Liming was launched at the West Fort at 4:30 PM yesterday. In order to save costs, the Shipyard did not invite outsiders to visit. The two ships are each 80 feet long, 13 feet wide, 3 feet deep, and have a displacement of 100 tons. Their speed is 11 nautical miles per hour. It is said that they will be completed in the spring of next year.

City Party Headquarters Designates Labor Arbitration Committee Members 118

Zhu Xuefan and Twenty-Four Others

Silk Cocoon Industry Cables to Request Retention of Jiangsu Industry Department 119

The Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Silk Cocoon Industry General Association and the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association cabled the National Government yesterday, saying: "To the National Government of Nanjing and the Jiangsu Provincial Government: It has been reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has decided to abolish the Jiangsu Industry Department, and all of its affiliated agencies will be closed within a year and reorganized. The matter concerns government orders, and the Provincial Government should have discretion. However, the official system is determined by the Central Government, and industry is at the forefront of public affairs. He Changzhi, governor of Jiangsu, has devoted himself to planning for the industry of this province and is especially concerned with maintaining silk cocoons. In recent years, silk cocoon varieties have been filled with inferior Japanese varieties, resulting in a gradual decline in the quality of cocoons produced. Since the establishment of the Jiangsu Provincial Seed Breeding Farm, various breeding farms have been happy to purchase its original seed. The establishment of the Jiangsu Provincial Cocoon Industry Suppression Office has also seriously suppressed the inferior varieties and made it impossible to sell them, all of which have benefited the industry of Jiangsu. It is clear that suppressing cocoon varieties and improving silk quality is just beginning to take shape, so why should it be suspended and abandon previous efforts? We implore your government to resolutely preside over the matter and withdraw the decision of the Jiangsu Provincial Government to abolish the Industry Department, so as to rectify silk cocoons and maintain the industry. We are extremely grateful for your fairness. The Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Cocoon Industry General Association Committee and the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association Committee respectfully knock."

National Lawyers Association Standing Committee Meeting 121

The Sixth Standing Committee Meeting of the National Lawyers Association was held in Yangzhou on the 16th of this month. Resolutions were made on cases, and a summary is as follows: (1) Regarding the unified legal rights case, it was resolved to recommend Standing Committee member Liu Liumin to draft a proposal for the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee. Resolutions of the Farmers Bank 122

Loan Policy for the Next Year

Since its establishment, the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank has regarded the improvement of rural areas and the support of the rural economy as its sole mission. Recently, in light of the changes in the social economy and the increasingly urgent need to support the rural economy, it was deemed necessary to have a detailed discussion on the bank's operations and loan policies. Therefore, in the middle of last month, a circular was sent to all branches throughout the province to draft future plans based on past experience. After the head office compiled and reviewed them, a meeting of all branch managers was convened at the Suzhou branch on December 18th. All branch managers attended and participated in the discussions. After detailed discussions, the loan policy for the 22nd year was decided, consisting of three items and seven sub-items. The decided items are recorded below: (A) Loan Nature: (1) Promoting Production: The goal of loans is to meet the needs of local production, such as improving varieties, selecting fertilizers, improving cultivation, introducing cooperation in new agricultural implements, preliminary manufacturing of agricultural products, marketing of agricultural products, promoting sideline occupations, etc. (2) Storing Agricultural Products: Regulating food supply, balancing market prices, and freeing farmers from the suffering of selling cheap and buying dear. (B) Loan Methods: This bank supports the rural economy by reforming rural organizations. In the 22nd year, this bank should focus on guiding farmers to organize various cooperatives and other beneficial organizations. The loan method should be based on the following items: (1) Cooperatives, (2) Warehouses, (3) Other organizations that directly or indirectly benefit farmers. (C) Loan Interest Rate: (1) Loans to cooperatives shall not exceed 1% per month. (2) Other loans shall be handled according to local conditions, financial seasons, and discretionary circumstances.

Japanese Ships Expel Chinese Seamen 123

The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun reports that the Japanese Seamen's Union, in order to secure the livelihoods of unemployed Japanese sailors, has decided to expel all Chinese sailors working on Japanese ships. Following the Dalian Steamship Company's plans to lay off staff, 46 Chinese crew members, including sailors and deckhands, from the Nissho Maru and Tenho Maru, both owned by the Nishinomiya Azuma Steamship Company, were all expelled when the ships entered Osaka Port at 1:00 PM on the 12th. On the other hand, 21 Japanese, including Chief Sailor Sasaki, were assigned to the Tenho Maru, and 21, including Chief Sailor Hanamura, were assigned to the Nissho Maru.

French Consul-General Issues Notice Prohibiting New Year's Gifts 125

The French Concession authorities, in view of the fact that residents within the concession often present large amounts of gifts to the Consul-General, the Board of Directors, and police officers during the New Year, believe that although this is a common human custom, the recipients are public officials, which is clearly contrary to the law. The French authorities believe that this bad habit needs to be actively improved and hereby notify all residents within the concession not to give any more gifts in the future, and also warn all subordinate officials to comply.

Inland Tap Water Company Loans for Installation 126

Measures after Stopping Retail Delivery

The Shanghai Inland Tap Water Company plans to stop the retail delivery method in separate areas and on a regular basis. The northeastern and southern districts (i.e., the city and the 16th pier) are scheduled to implement this from January of the 22nd year. The company, in view of the fact that the general public may not be able to afford to install water pipes for the time being, fears inconvenience, so it plans to implement a loan installation method to promote its popularity. It is heard that the outline of this method has been approved by the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau. Those within the company's water supply area where road pipes have arrived but have not yet connected to tap water can refer to the outline at the company and entrust a registered plumbing shop to apply for installation and repay the installation fee in installments to enjoy clean water. This is a good method that is easy to implement.

No. 10 Public Bus to Be Divided into Three Sections 128

The China General Omnibus Company, in order to meet the needs of the public, petitioned the Public Works Department to divide the No. 10 public bus route into three sections: (1) The western section runs from Wujiaochang, via Connaught Road, Xinzha Road, Beijing Road, to the Bund. When returning, it takes Suzhou Road, Sichuan Road, and makes a flat circle, then re-enters Beijing Road and returns to Wujiaochang. (2) The middle section runs from the intersection of Beijing Road and Tibet Road to Huishan Road and back. (3) The eastern section runs from the Bund via Seward Road and Ward Road to Linqing Road and back. When turning around on the Bund, it goes via Beijing Road, Sichuan Road, and Suzhou Road to Waibaidu Bridge. The company's intention is that the bus used to run the entire route (from Wujiaochang to Linqing Road), but tickets were sold in three sections. The adjustment of the number of passengers in each section and the increase or decrease in the number of vehicles was inconvenient. Therefore, it is proposed to run in sections to cope with the situation. After consideration by the Chief of the Police Department, it was believed that the proposed eastern section, running from the Bund via Beijing Road, Sichuan Road, and Suzhou Road, required three right turns, which would be very inconvenient during busy hours. It is possible to turn around on the Bund Xin Road (heavy vehicle road), which only requires one right turn at the Jiujiang Road intersection. The company stated that it was willing to follow this method, and the Public Works Department has temporarily approved it. Whether there is insurance or hindrance in turning around at the Jiujiang Road intersection in the eastern section is still under consideration by the Police Department.

New Year's Cards and Invitations

To Ensure Swift Delivery

Must Be Bundled Separately

The Shanghai Postal Authorities say that with the end of the year approaching, the congestion of mailing New Year's cards, etc., is inevitable. If the sender has invitations, etc., it is best to mail them separately from New Year's cards. As for New Year's cards to be mailed to this city or domestically or internationally, if they can be bundled into bundles separately and then mailed, delivery will definitely be faster.

Unfortunate News Arrives Causing Mental Breakdown Leading to Suicide by Poisoning 129

A Fatal Telegram

Shop in Hometown Closed

Wang Yimei, a native of Fujian, over forty years old, who worked in lacquerware, brought a large batch of goods to Shanghai from his hometown on the 4th of this month to sell, lodging at No. 58 Jisheng Inn, Fujian Road, Sima Road. The day before yesterday (the 18th), his wife gave him a telegram, saying that the shop at home had suddenly been ordered to close by the troops stationed there, and asked him to return home quickly. After receiving the telegram, Wang was stunned, panicked, and temporarily lost his mind. He had the idea of dying. Last night, he secretly smoked raw opium to commit suicide. The waiter noticed and immediately sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at 10:35 PM. The body was transferred from the hospital to the morgue for examination.

Appeal from Pudong Ferry Operators 131

Ferry Terminal Issues

Lu Baokui and others from the Pudong Lannidu Ferry Business Office again submitted a document to the Municipal Government, stating: A re-submission urgently requests clear instructions. [We] respectfully received Directive No. 539 from your office, which stated: We have learned that the cross-river ferry between Dongmen Road and Dongchang Road operated by the city is different from the route of the ferry operators and is not related. The request for relief should not be considered. This reply, etc., respectfully notes that the city ferry and the ferry route are different and not related. It shows that your office is determined to carry out construction and does not lose the purpose of benefiting the people. Baokui and others have personally benefited from this and admire it. However, there is still something that must be clearly stated to your office. That is, the Jiangtian Wharf in Puxi and Dongmen Road are the berths for the ferry and the city ferry and are very close to each other. Although the routes are different, the business is affected. The public wharf in Lannidu is privately owned by the Yu family and must be abolished. Now the Dongchang Wharf has been designated by the Public Utilities Bureau as the city ferry terminal. The Lannidu Wharf has been widened by four zhang to the north and south. As a result of negotiations, once abolished, Baokui and others' ferry and the city ferry will inevitably take the same path. There will be no room for the ferry to stand. It will be abolished without being abolished, which is inevitable. Baokui and the other 37 households and hundreds of boatmen are on the verge of losing their livelihoods, and the public is panicking and cannot live in peace. The different routes and unrelated nature are only a way to seek temporary relief and are contrary to the current facts. It is still not enough to allay public concerns. For this reason, we again urge your office to clearly state the existence or abolition of Lannidu, and how Baokui and others' ferry terminal will be designated for relief after the abolition, in order to answer public doubts and alleviate worries.

Kidnapper Who Guarded Hostage in Liu Nianchun Case Arrested 134

Liu Nianchun, the owner of Dingkang Gold Store on Tianjin Road, lived on North Chengdu Road. At 6:30 PM on September 13th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, Liu was returning to his residence from the store in his own car. When he arrived at the alley entrance and was about to get out of the car, he was suddenly kidnapped by three bandits who drove the driver off. The bandits drove the car and kidnapped Liu to a bandit's hideout at No. 30, Lane [Name], Tang [Name] Lane, South Pier, and monitored him. They then sent a letter to Liu's family, demanding a huge sum of money. Liu was later redeemed with a huge sum of money, and several kidnappers were arrested and executed. However, there was still one kidnapper, Yang Asi, from Tongzhou, who was responsible for guarding the hostage in the bandit's den at the time. He had been on the run for a long time and had not been arrested. Until about 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, Chinese detectives Xie Futang and Zhang Yunhong of the General Inspection Office of the General Patrol Room arrested Yang Asi in the Xinglu Lane on Broadway and took him to the patrol room for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Patrol Room lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the details of the case and requested that Yang be detained for investigation. After reviewing the confession, Judge Qian Wenji ordered Yang to be detained for another interrogation at a later date.

Extortion Resembling Kidnapping 135

Using a Car to Abduct Someone for $20

Li Yuzhong, a 46-year-old native of Funing, who lived in a thatched fence at No. 4 Zhongshan Road, west of the Tanziwan police station in the fourth district of Zhabei, was not yet awake at about 5:00 AM yesterday morning when a car arrived with five people on board. One person knocked on the door and entered, showed a pistol and handcuffs, and asked Li if he knew what was going on before putting Li Yuzhong in the car and driving away. Li's wife, Wang (29 years old), did not know what was going on, so she waited until about 1:00 PM before reporting to the Tanziwan police station, saying that her husband had been kidnapped by bandits. After receiving the report, Inspector Ge Weirui immediately reported the situation to the Fourth District. District Chief Liu Shirong and District Member Gou Zhixin were preparing to send detectives Xie Qihua and others to investigate when they received a phone call from the Tanziwan police station reporting that Li Yuzhong had been released. District Member Gou and others, considering that the case was bizarre, immediately ordered Inspector Ge and others to summon Li Yuzhong and Li Yushi to the case for questioning. According to Li Yuzhong, he had previously partnered with Chong Guanting and others in business and still owed Chong and others $20. That morning, Chong Guanting and his brother Chongfu, as well as three people whose names he did not know, brought pistols and handcuffs to abduct him to a small teahouse near the Li Road Bridge in the southern city to demand money. It was then mediated and $10 was paid to settle the matter. He did not know that his wife had reported to the Tanziwan police station in your district. After reviewing the confession, the magistrate ruled that carrying a pistol to extort money was too outrageous. If Wang had falsely reported a kidnapping, she should also be punished. However, the defendant had not been brought to justice and could not be verified. Therefore, it was ruled that he should be sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Hostage Escapes and Returns to Dongshan 136

To Inform Fellow Villagers from Dongting in Shanghai

The Yutai steamboat, belonging to the Gongmao Shipping Bureau in this city, which travels between Suzhou and Dongting Dongshan, was intercepted by bandits in the middle of the voyage. The escorting water police were shot and wounded, and passengers were killed. Passengers Xi Chunqiao, Zhou Yinggao, and others were kidnapped before leaving. The Gongmao Shipping Bureau and the Dongting Dongshan Native Association in Shanghai telegraphed various military and police agencies, requesting suppression of the bandits, as has been reported in this newspaper. It has now been learned that the kidnapped hostage, Xi Chunqiao, is the manager of the Dalun Silk and Satin Bureau in this city, and Zhou Yinggao is an employee of the Tiancheng Silk and Satin Bureau. Both are from Dongting Dongshan. They were traveling together from Suzhou on the same ship to return home. After being kidnapped, Zhu Xianhuai, chairman of the Dongting Dongshan Native Association in Shanghai, in addition to submitting reports to the provincial government and other agencies requesting suppression, also traveled by car to Suzhou from Shanghai the next day to rescue them. Yesterday, the association received a telegram from Chairman Zhu from Suzhou stating that both hostages, Xi Chunqiao and Zhou Yinggao, had safely escaped at the same time the night before and had returned to their homes in Dongshan. Please inform fellow villagers in Shanghai.

(Resolution) Pass the review; (X) Cancel the physician's prescription kickbacks and organize new medicine measures. (Resolution) Submit to the Standing Committee for continued discussion; (XI) Whether the association's "New Medicine and Society" will still be published with the Shishi Xinbao's seven daily newspapers. Counterfeit Aspirin Case 142

Sentencing Next Tuesday

Taihe Western Medicine Company, located at 7 Sanhe Lane, Sichuan Road, was found to be counterfeiting and selling aspirin from the German company Bayer. The Shanghai manager of Defu Foreign Company discovered this and reported it to the police. The police found more than a hundred packages of counterfeit medicine. The manager, Hu Heping, was not at the store at the time, so his younger brother, Hu Hede, was arrested and sent to the First District Court. After Judge Zhang Junqing's hearing, he was released on 5,000 yuan bail, and the trial was adjourned to yesterday. First, the defendant's lawyer stated that the case was adjourned, and both parties had reached a settlement, requesting the court to dismiss the case. However, the plaintiffs' lawyers, Wu Linkun and Wang Fuchang, stated that the settlement was true, but the counterfeiting of medicines was also true. Whether or not a crime has been committed should be made clear. If the court gives an opportunity for rehabilitation and leniently handles the case, they would not object. The police lawyer, Qian Xun'er, stated that the public prosecution cannot be withdrawn under the law, but since both parties have now reached a settlement and the defendant has repented, they requested a lenient sentence. When asked, the representative of Defu Foreign Company, lawyer Wei, also expressed his request that the court give a lenient sentence or grant probation. Judge Zhang then adjourned the case for sentencing next Monday.

▲Double Fish Brand National Hot Water Bottle: Most hot water bottles among daily necessities come from abroad. Recently, it has been heard that a certain gentleman, in order to restore profit rights, raised huge funds to establish the Danhua Industrial Factory, and manufactured pure national Double Fish brand hot water bottles. Mass production and mass supply. The shape and quality of this hot water bottle are first-class, enough to compete with foreign goods. Reader's Consultant

Discussion on the Questions Raised by Mr. Bao Zhizheng (II) 151

--Original letter see this column on the 17th of this month

Mr. Jiang CunSong's information: ㈠The active way to deal with the Public Security Bureau is to unite with the industry and ask the party headquarters for assistance, in order to achieve the purpose of punishing the Public Security Bureau that extorts the people. The passive way is to appeal to the public opinion and ask for unanimous assistance. ㈡Regarding the issue of making a living, you can ask local people to hold a meeting to discuss relief measures. If this request is not met, you will naturally have to make a living on your own; if you can't find a legitimate job, then "openly and boldly" continue to do your old business. Since the country doesn't feed you, why bother about whether it is legal or illegal? If you are arrested by the government for this reason, then everyone will go to jail together, anyway there is food to eat. In short, if everyone is not timid and united, there is no way not to get the final victory!

Mr. Chen Yingjie's information: I am a young man who dropped out of school. I used to study in middle school; later, because of the stubbornness of my family, I was forced to drop out of school. At that time, I was driven by the desire to study and also made strong resistance, but in the end, because my heart was long and my strength was short, I succumbed and obeyed the strict order to go into business, but this is completely different from my temperament, so I have no interest and no vitality. However, my desire for knowledge has not diminished at all. When I am free in the morning and evening, I study hard at my desk, and I especially enjoy browsing books and newspapers. After several years, on the recommendation of a friend, I took a job in the academic world. As a result of my serious and arduous work, I was relied on by the school authorities, and it has been more than four years now. However, in recent years, the number of unemployed people in society has increased, and there are more people than positions. Even the small primary school rice bowl is in danger of being snatched away. Unfortunately, I was also among those who were rejected this year. Because of this, I am panicked in spirit and materially, and I have no solution. I have become a pitiful person who has dropped out of school and is unemployed. Every time I ask a friend to find a work-study opportunity, it is impossible. According to the current phenomenon, doing things must talk about "qualifications," and qualifications cannot be bought without "money"! Then, since I have little money and lack qualifications, how will I stand in society in the future? Unequal society, unfortunate life, please give me a bright indication!

Reply: We express our deepest sympathy for your fighting spirit. The "qualification" problem is indeed a kind of pain felt by many young people who have dropped out of school in modern times. We say fairly, the restriction of qualifications is to prevent the abuse of registration, indirectly to maintain the uniformity of the effectiveness of handling affairs, and not only to ask "qualifications" but not "real learning," the original intention is not too harsh; However, ordinary people often only value the virtual name of qualifications, without investigating the reality, and the value of qualifications is fundamentally lost. In fact, in our opinion, the current qualification restrictions are also limited. You see how many unqualified people rely on their bare-handed struggle and have also achieved considerable success; and how many people who have neither qualifications nor real learning rely on the "promotion" of their relatives and friends, and they will actually be among the "noble and prominent." Where is the restriction of qualifications? It's just fooling a group of poor kids! We certainly don't want to learn from the latter group of people to "flatter and run a camp," the fighting spirit of the former is indeed worthy of being our model! Therefore, what we can contribute here is only the word "struggle." Is society unfair? We must struggle! Is life unfortunate? We must struggle! "Man can definitely overcome nature." We must use continuous efforts to break through all the current difficulties: I don't believe that all the current darkness can ultimately overwhelm our courageous youth! The light is in front of us, let's rush forward!

Mr. Ding Jiean's information: ㈠We are born in this muddy society. The temptations and pressures from the outside world are so severe. How can we continue to maintain our personality and not be assimilated into the vulgar customs? ㈡Life is always inevitable to have times of sorrow and pain. When this situation comes to our heads, how can we prevent ourselves from being decadent? ㈢If we want to accomplish a career or learning, we must go through many twists and turns and difficulties. How can we not shrink back halfway?

Reply: Although the questions in the letter are divided into three items, the reason is only one point, that is, the issue of personal "will." If a person has an extremely strong will, no matter what difficult blows and evil temptations, they will not make him succumb; conversely, if a person has no will, then everything is impossible to talk about, and in the end, they can only go with the flow. There will never be any success! As for the cultivation of will, it must of course rely on one's own cultivation. On weekdays, whenever something comes to hand, we should first conduct a detailed observation, judge its right and wrong, and once right and wrong are determined, we should hold on to the courage to proceed, regardless of any difficulties in front of us. This great courage is "will." To have this courage, first, we must recognize the true nature of the universe and life clearly, and second, we must have a strict distinction between the concepts of profit and harm; generally speaking, it is to have a "broad vision." People with short-sightedness will never have any "will." To sum it up again, the explanation of will is "not afraid" and "not confused." If a person can be "not afraid" and "not confused," they can also deal with everything.

Jiangsu Provincial Education Department Promotes Livelihood Education 156

Plans to Take Over Various Affiliated Institutions of the Former Industry Department

Striving to Integrate Production and Education

Zhou Fohai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department, attaches great importance to livelihood education and considers it one of the central tasks of the department. The plan to improve livelihood education is also being carefully studied. Now, because the Jiangsu Industry Department has been abolished, many of its affiliated institutions, such as provincial and county farms and factories, can be used for education. Therefore, in order to increase the efficiency of vocational education in schools and to popularize livelihood education among the general public, it is heard that Director Zhou has obtained the consent of the chairman and plans to take over the affiliated institutions of the former Industry Department that can be used for education and put them under the jurisdiction of the Education Department, so that various vocational schools, social education institutions, and county junior and senior primary schools can make full use of them, striving to integrate production and education and achieve the effect of livelihood education. Currently, the nature, content, location, funding, and other items of various affiliated institutions are being investigated. After the investigation is completed and the proposal is submitted to the provincial government for approval, they will be taken over separately. How to reorganize and how to use them after the takeover is a pioneering initiative in education, and the department is also carefully studying and planning in detail.

Hunan Province Holds Middle School Graduation Joint Examination 157

About 4,000 Students Participating in the Examination

Four Days Starting from January 16

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province attaches great importance to the joint graduation examination for students. In the first semester of this year, a joint graduation examination for high school students was held once, which yielded great results. Now, it is found that this semester is about to end, and there are more than 3,000 graduates from junior high school and more than 100 graduates from high school, who urgently need to continue to hold the examination. Therefore, the Provincial Government Committee decided to establish a "Hunan Provincial Middle School Student Graduation Joint Examination Committee," and recommended He Jian as the chairman, Zhu Jingnong as the vice chairman, and Luo Dafan, Huang Shiheng, Huang Jiasheng, Wang Taizhong, Xia Kaiquan, Yang Naikang, Duan Bijiang, Luo Chuanju, Xie Zuyou, Jiang Lou, Ouyang Gangzhong, and others as committee members. The committee was immediately convened and mutually agreed to elect Ouyang Gangzhong, Xia Kaiquan, and Luo Dafan as standing committee members, and Xie Zuyou, Huang Jiasheng, Huang Shiheng, Wang Taizhong, and Jiang Lou as members of the performance evaluation and review committee. The joint examination date was set for January 16, 17, 18, and 19, 22. Students in the provincial capital will be directly handled by the committee, and all students in various counties will be organized by the committee to send personnel to jointly organize branches with the respective county governments and county education bureaus, and the test questions will be drafted by the committee and strictly sealed and distributed to show caution. The Education Department has already notified the principals of various schools to quickly send the list of graduating students for numbering, and the joint examination measures have been drafted and submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for approval and have been promulgated for implementation.

Preliminary Plan for Reforming Chinese Education Suggested by the League of Nations Education Inspection Group (Continued) 162

High Quality Improvements Should be Made to Higher Education

Foreign Textbooks Should Disappear from Secondary Schools

(B) Secondary education should not only be a preparation for entering university, because only a small portion of secondary school graduates can go on to higher education. Vocational schools and normal schools actually constitute an indispensable part of secondary education. The strength of normal school graduates can ensure the unity of primary and secondary education. Vocational education must be emphasized and further developed, so that students with talent can rise from lower-level vocational education to the highest level. (C) Higher education should be greatly improved in quality. There are too many universities in various cultural centers. On average, five students require a fully learned teacher to spend all or part of their time, which is unreasonable. If several competing universities in one location cannot be completely unified, then strive for their cooperation to curb wasteful competition. Private universities or specialized schools that do not adhere to this cooperation to support a national, efficient education system should not be allowed to be established.

(IV) Efficient Teaching. (A) All teachers must be proficient in the subjects they teach, not just in their teaching methods. Basic education in history and psychology is valuable, but should not neglect the teaching materials themselves because of such studies. (B) Lectures should be based less on textbooks and more on experiments and practical work (especially in science) and reference books (in history and language). (C) The number of lecture hours in all schools should be reduced, and the number of hours in laboratories and manual work should be increased comparatively. (D) Specialized terminology in science should be standardized. Foreign textbooks should disappear from secondary schools. This is necessary. The study of European languages (such as English) must enable graduates of general courses in secondary schools to use modern scientific texts in universities. Establishing specialized scientific terminology in Chinese is a most urgent task that the Ministry of Education should promote (a special committee should be organized by hiring European experts). (E) The government should ensure that all scientific institutions are fully equipped with instruments manufactured in China. These instruments can be manufactured by private or public factories.

Preliminary Plans in Urgent Need. (I) A special committee should be sent to Europe as soon as possible to study the organization of school administration in European countries. The personnel sent should be experienced people, and they should be expected to be the leaders of the transformation in the future. We believe that Chinese experts who are familiar with the situation and educational administration methods in Europe are more beneficial than inviting European experts to come to Nanjing. However, if the Ministry of Education wants to obtain a competent educational administrator from Europe as an assistant, the League of Nations will be willing to help find a competent expert. This person should not only have been trained in a certain part of educational administration, but must also have broad and thorough practical experience. If such an expert can come to China, he should be at the disposal of the Chinese government at any time to assist in everything, for a period of at least one year. (II) We further suggest that China should send experts to Europe to study teaching materials, curriculum, etc. (III) The investigations that must be carried out locally in the areas selected for the first pilot projects of compulsory education should be prepared in time, and publicity to the public must be carried out to prepare psychologically in order to eliminate illiteracy. (IV) The necessary regulations for various administrative committees should be drafted immediately, and the Ministry of Education should appoint leaders from the academic and other fields to organize a university administrative meeting to discuss plans for reforming university education. (V) The problem of determining specialized scientific terminology should be studied immediately. (End)

Family Education Lecture Broadcast 167

Yesterday, Liu Zhanen, the president of Soochow University, gave a lecture at the Dadong Bookstore's Family Education Lecture series. The topic was "Family Education and Civic Education." The main points are roughly divided into four points: ⑴ Family education is national salvation education. ⑵ Family education should take civic education as the center. ⑶ Family education should be integrated with civic education. ⑷ The implementation method of family education should be to organize family civic training groups as the main body, and detailed his own implementation in the family, so that each family knows what to learn from. Tomorrow, Wang Zhiwei, a master of education from the University of California, will give a lecture.

Wonderful Performance of West Qing Basketball

Hujiang Defeats St. John's 176

| Result: 57 to 35 |

| St. John's Lost Because Their Attackers Could Not Defend |

| Soochow Wins West Qing (Group B) |

Relying on their agile figures and superb skills, the Hujiang athletes were able to defeat the St. John's basketball team with a score of 57 to 35 in yesterday's West Qing Group A game. At that time, more than 100 Hujiang students, both male and female, sat around, cheering and shouting, singing together, and their joy was almost indescribable. After the game, the Group B Soochow vs. West Qing game followed, and as a result, Soochow won 42 to 27. Soochow led 19 to 16 in the first half.

Frequent Whistles 177

St. John's and Hujiang are long-time rivals in the basketball world. In recent years, St. John's players have left the school one after another, and their strength has been weaker. Hujiang is the opposite. With elite troops and sufficient supplies, they are invincible. At the beginning of the fierce battle, they were anxious and their hands did not follow their commands. Either they went too far or they did not reach the goal. The sound of free throws was frequently heard, and the warriors were frightened. Chen Xianglong committed the first foul, and Hujiang's Sun Baoqing scored the first point. Hujiang's Tao Zunan followed, committing a foul again and again, and Qian Jingyong also got a point. In the blink of an eye, Hujiang's Cheng Jingsheng, a surprise soldier, came out of the gate, shooting a basket diagonally. Chen Xianglong charged into the battle alone. After waiting for him to retreat, he was supported from behind. The Hujiang army was calm and powerful, soaring straight down, and in less than ten minutes, they led by 11 to 2.

Handling with Ease 178

Turning to this battle, driving a light car and taking a familiar road, the balls of both sides flowed into the basket like shooting stars, unlike the previous failed attempts. The anxiety had disappeared, and they were handling it with ease. Almost every minute and every second, they all had the opportunity to build achievements. In comparison, if St. John's scored a ball, Hujiang would retaliate with a follow-up shot, and sometimes even added interest. St. John's three forwards were good at shooting baskets, and the inner guard Sun Baoqing also strongly supported them. Invisibly, Hujiang had already taken the upper hand. At the end of the first half, Hujiang was 27 and St. John's was 14.

Honorable Retirement 179

Starting the second half, St. John's was very brilliant. The whole army fought together, and the attack and defense corresponded to each other. The reason for St. John's previous defeat was that the forwards could not take care of the defense. The inner guards Wu Youliang and Tao Zunan had increased responsibilities, and often used the strength of two people to jointly resist the activities of the five tigers. The contribution of Wu and Tao was the crown of the whole team. Not long after the battle, Tao first made a remarkable contribution, scoring a ball and hitting a free throw, and Hou Xuemin also won two more points. Five points had been obtained, and St. John's had a million appearances, and victory was in sight. At that time, Tao was sent off the field with four penalties. Tao retired honorably and could be said to be without shame, but the team's sharpness gradually declined and it was difficult to recover.

Deserved Reputation 180

Three Special Points of Shanghai College: Quick Dribbling, Accurate Throwing, Excellent Teamwork. This is Where St. John's Falls Short. Although St. John's Sometimes Came Close, They Gradually Fell Behind. Artistry Has Its Highs and Lows. In the First Ten Minutes, St. John's Scored More Points Than Shanghai College. However, Over Time, Shanghai College Relied on Their Strengths and Rose Steadily. The Scoreboard Showed a Significant Difference. In the End, Shanghai College Won 57 to 35. Referees: Shu Hong, Li Zuqi

Jiujiang Basketball Championship 186

Zi Qiang Team Wins Group A Championship

Nan Xun Team Wins Group B Championship

(Jiujiang Correspondence) Jiujiang's sports scene has long been considered dull, and past results have been extremely poor. Since Long Zexian came to Xun, he has vigorously promoted sports, and the atmosphere has gradually become more enthusiastic. Whenever there is an important competition, the audience always exceeds one thousand people. This time, Long Zexian, the sports director of the Provincial Fourth Middle School, joined forces with Zhu Chuikai and Huang Yi to jointly launch the Jiujiang Winter Basketball Championship. On the one hand, it promotes sports throughout the city, and on the other hand, the ticket proceeds are donated to the Northeastern Volunteer Army. A total of ten teams participated in this competition, divided into Group A and Group B, with five teams in each group. The competition method adopted a knockout system. The winner of the final in Group A was the Si Zhong Zi Qiang team, a perennial winner in the city, and the Qiang Hua team, organized by most of Jiujiang's sports enthusiasts. The winners of the final in Group B were the Jiujiang Railway Bureau Team B and the Lian Xi Vocational School. The finals were held at the Provincial Fourth Middle School basketball court at 3 PM on the 17th. As a result, the championship in Group A was won by the Provincial Fourth Middle School Zi Qiang team, and the championship in Group B was won by the Nanxun Railway Bureau Team B. The results were satisfactory and represent a good phenomenon for inland sports. The details of the competition are as follows:

Finals Snippets 187

In the Group B final, the Nanxun B athletes were tall and strong, and fiercely contested for the ball. The Lianxi players were small and thin, and were outmatched. As a result, Nanxun B won. The Group A final followed, with Huang Song as the referee. The atmosphere was exceptionally tense. The Zi Qiang team is known as a perennial winner in Jiujiang, and their passing and shooting are excellent. The Qiang Hua team is made up entirely of sports teachers, and their experience is not inferior to that of Zi Qiang. Unfortunately, their coordination was lacking. The result of the first half was 22 to 8. Although the Qiang Hua forwards were very valiant, the Zi Qiang defenders were tight and impenetrable. As a result, Zi Qiang won 47 to 31. The basketball championship, which caused a sensation in the city, came to a successful conclusion.

Silver Dollar Market Nearing the End of the Year 198

Yesterday, from the external observation of financial business, nearing the end of the year, various 款項 urgently need to be summarized. The busyness of the procedures goes without saying. However, since new transactions are not many, and previous accounts are being sorted out, most are shrinking to prevent market instability, so it is still not as prosperous as in previous years. Therefore, even if this year-end is busy, it is feared that it will not be as intense as in previous years. As for the various prices of interest rates, dismantling and auxiliary currency, the morning and afternoon markets were the same.

Only Financial Short-Term Bonds Rebound by Four Yuan

Yesterday (20th), the market situation of various bonds on the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange was still very quiet. The market sentiment has not yet turned around, and although the price rebounded compared to the previous day, the rise and fall were peaceful. The total transaction volume before and after the market was 5.57 million yuan. Regarding the changes, the rise of the 20-year financial short-term bonds was extremely strong. Actual demand for cotton yarn is increasingly sluggish due to tight financial conditions. Various merchant groups have also turned to stagnation. The yarn market in Guangdong and other places is poor, hence the market is depressed. The initial enthusiasm is gradually dissipating. However, some still have interest in going long due to the rise in raw cotton prices. It is said that Rongxing will close out a large number of long positions this month.

Raw cotton prices suddenly rose in the second and third sessions, driving the yarn market up, but the closing was soft again. Near-month contracts fell 1.24 qian, while far-month contracts were flat. Recent Cotton Shows Slackness 209

Manufacturers have confirmed purchasing coarse cotton in producing areas.

The cotton market is fluctuating and uncertain, rising and falling abruptly, leaving people confused. However, general speculators believe that domestic cotton production is insufficient for factory use, and the prices of Indian and American cotton are difficult to come to Shanghai due to the influence of precious metals. Therefore, most are inclined to purchase cotton. However, a certain manufacturer in Tianjin and Shandong production areas has indeed purchased 4,000 bales of coarse-grade cotton, which have already been loaded onto ships and are being transported to Shanghai. Therefore, the market conditions in the near term have shown slight slackness.

In the afternoon, it was heard that current cotton demand was healthy, and the market was pulled up by multiple parties. Market sentiment suddenly tightened, and each month rose by 2.34 qian. Tianjin Merchants Actively Seek Spot Flour 213

丨150,000 to 160,000 Bags Transacted Yesterday丨

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for all months were slightly weak due to the large amount of foreign wheat purchased by various large and small factories in recent days, which has satisfied their appetite. Foreign merchants are still actively selling. Yesterday, the price of foreign wheat also decreased slightly, and the appetite of Dalian merchants also temporarily stopped. Therefore, market sentiment was downward. However, in the afternoon, Tianjin merchants suddenly came to the market to actively seek recent and spot flour, with a strong appetite. 150,000 to 160,000 bags of spot and near-term flour were transacted on the day, and the market was immediately lifted. Before closing, it triggered short covering by floating long and scattered short positions, and market sentiment was even better. Due to demand exceeding supply, the price has risen by half an angle compared to the previous day. There has been no import or export of foreign rice for a long time, and there are still 450,000 bags in stock, all in the hands of foreign merchants. 3,000 bags were transferred last week, and the market is still in a dismissed situation.

Oil Market

Hankou Telegram Shows Bai Tong Oil Falling 221

Bai Tong Oil's market is fluctuating, and rises and falls have not exceeded 2, which has been the case for months since the new oil was produced. Sometimes it is lively, and sometimes it is weak, but still has no great development. Distributors in other ports handled a batch of Zhejiang road earlier. Recently, settlement has been due, so those transported by train in recent days are purchases of futures settled previously, not the current market transaction. The price seems to be slightly weaker than before, and usually only rises and falls by a few jiao. The future forward price was between 23.24 yuan and 23 yuan per 砠, while recently it has been between 22.56 yuan. According to Zhejiang road oil mills, they are unwilling to reduce prices further due to cost reasons, and the situation seems to be stabilizing. However, according to a telegram from Hankou the day before yesterday, the source of Xiang Tong is strong, and prices have fallen to 13 taels per customer. The Hankou market is cheaper than the Zhejiang market. Compared to the current market, Hankou Tong oil is cheaper than Zhejiang Tong oil. Local distributors in this port have already abandoned Hankou and switched to Zhejiang in recent years. Now that Hankou Tong oil is already calculated, perhaps this can change the line of sight again, abandoning Zhejiang and switching to Hankou is also within expectations. If Zhejiang Tong oil can be affected by Hankou, and prices fall accordingly, then buyers will always choose the cheaper option.

Free Talk

Lotus Fall (2) 245

— Mu Shiying

"Not hungry? Such a big man eating so little."

"Not hungry. How come you're here all alone?"

"The whole family is dead." Her eyelids reddened, and she wanted to cry again. I quickly kept silent, and after a while, when she was better, I said, "What happened?"

"They fought, and wiped out my whole family."

"Where are you going?"

"Where can I go?"

"Where are you planning to run?"

"I wasn't planning on running anywhere. I took a few pancakes, and ran all the way here. What about you?"

"I didn't even bring food. Not getting killed by the soldiers is already great luck. How can I plan where to run? I'll just go wherever I can."

At that time, she and I sat closer and closer together. I waved my hand and touched her hand. I smiled, and moved my body a little, very embarrassed.

"You should still sit further away?"

So I moved away a bit, sitting far apart talking.

It was really getting late. The stars in the sky were so dense, pushing each other, as if trying to push someone down. The grass outside the pavilion was all wet with dew, and a few upside-down trees in the distance stretched their branches towards the moon. A gust of wind blew, and I felt a little cold. Outside the pavilion, a night bird cried out, its voice strange enough, like a ghost crying, making one's heart cold, followed by a gust of wind. She shrank her neck and shivered. I glanced at her.

"You should still sit closer?" she said.

"Are you cold?"

"I'm scared."

I moved over and sat down next to her. Just as I touched her body, she flinched and said, "You won't..." Looking at me.

I shook my head.

So she leaned on me and said, "I'm tired!"

And closed her eyes.

I looked at her, and all my fatigue and loneliness disappeared. I thought, I am not living in the world alone, I am with her in this pavilion—we are two people.

The next day, she had flushed cheeks and disheveled eyebrows. The virginity in her eyes was stolen by a thief last night. She looked at the sky, looked at the sun, and then looked at me, and suddenly covered her face and cried. I didn't dare to say anything. I knew I had done something wrong. She cried for a long time before raising her head and pointing her finger at my nose and saying, "It's all you!"

I lowered my head.

"You said you wouldn't."

"I didn't expect it."

"Elegance" and "Vulgarity" 246

— Du Heng

Recently, there has been a trend in literary works of using a large amount of vulgar language, as if it is not enough to show populism without it. The so-called vulgar language here of course specifically refers to that curse that involves a woman's particular organ, namely the Shanghai phrase "Nao Niang" (pronounced like "Na Niang") and the various derivations of the same phrase in other places. Originally, for the sake of conveying the spirit of spoken language, using a few of them appropriately is not only permissible but also necessary; but using them in excessive amounts, even in narratives, in descriptions, and even in poems, then it implicitly becomes a promotion. This kind of promotion, even if it cannot be said to be particularly undesirable, is at least as particularly undesirable as promoting "national essence." Using phrases like "Nao Niang" to curse people, gradually the curser no longer considers it a significant insult, and the cursed person seems to be able to handle it calmly. Thus, there are cases of cursing a son but actually not cursing at all, and cases of cursing siblings without feeling "incestuous," and even more gradually, this cursing simply ceases to be cursing. It is merely regarded as a kind of exclamation mark in speech, used to emphasize tone. This is really because our popular spoken vocabulary lacks a word that can be used to emphasize tone. Something can be bad to the extent of "Nao Niang," and at the same time it can be good to the extent of "Nao Niang": if this is still cursing, then it is simply firing blanks. In short, it has become a phrase with sound but without meaning.

It is indeed common to use these words frequently in popular spoken language, but we also feel that it is not necessary to tack one onto every sentence; even if there are people who tack one onto every sentence, they are ultimately not the majority. Those who use it the most are still our writers. The reason is probably because our writers feel that these words are very striking, so they always grab it as the unique feature of popular spoken language.

Opposite to "vulgar" is "elegant." I think the most elegant spoken language should be that of people from Beiping.

This elegance is also partly politeness. Indeed, anyone who has been to a Beiping restaurant must imagine that China is the most polite nation. However, this restaurant-style politeness may not be purely politeness, and contains a hint of "small change," so it is not very reliable. Then I can cite another example.

For example, if a rickshaw with passengers wants to overtake a rickshaw without passengers, then the rickshaw driver will say "Lao Jia" (excuse me). As for things like the person in the back bumping into the front and then cursing the person in front for "not having eyes," that kind of thing is generally unheard of.

"Lao Jia" is a very common phrase in northern spoken language, yet it is very elegant. There is no way to say it using less elegant words; the forced translation would be "With your chariot's toil." "Jia" is derived from horse, and in ancient China, the most common means of transportation was horse-drawn carriage, so it can be seen that this phrase has been around for a long time. Entrusting you to do something means asking you to sit in your chariot to do it, how courteous.

The "Lao Jia" in the mouth of a rickshaw driver can of course be interpreted as "With your chariot's toil," but from the point of view of the "Jia" character being derived from "horse," then this polite phrase has become no less of an insult than "Nao Niang." The rickshaw drivers do not think of "Lao Jia" as asking people to sit in a horse-drawn carriage, but as asking people to "Jia" the rickshaw like a horse—that kind of "toil." Therefore, this elegant word, it can be said, is just like that vulgar word, people only remember the sound and forget the meaning.

Our ideal language is one that neither uses "Lao Jia" to replace "Please move aside," nor uses "Nao Niang" to replace...replace what?

Replace everything.

Random Jests by Bao Qiao 247

— Shi Zhecun

Bao Qiao (Poggis), an Italian satirist of the 14th century, born in 1380, authored a volume of humorous anecdotes, a genre quite similar to our country's "Laughing Grove Wide Records," mocking clerics, literati, noblewomen, and wealthy merchants with concise wit. While some jokes are ribald, they are not obscene. In literature, there is a special talent for this kind of work. In England, it's Swift (Swift), in France, Voltaire, and Rabelais. In our country, Li Yu of the Lake, is a comparable figure. Now, I have transcribed and translated several anecdotes by Bao to entertain the readers.

A noblewoman, whose husband was an ambassador, had been away for a long time. One day, a postman asked her if she had any letters to send to her husband. She replied, "How can you expect me to write letters when my husband took his pen with him, leaving only an empty inkwell at home?"

A man living in the city of Cu Piao, named John, was troubled because he couldn't figure out a way to detect if his wife was having an affair. Later, after racking his brains, he came up with a brilliant plan. He castrated himself! This way, if his wife were to have a child, then she must have committed adultery.

In the village of Biergola, a mountain man was about to marry a girl from his neighbor's house, but after carefully examining her, he claimed that the girl was too delicate and too young, and he refused to marry her. But her dull-witted father retorted, "She has grown up so much that you don't believe it, and the facts can prove it. She has already given birth to three children for the priest in our parish."

Prince Barnabo of Milan was very fond of women. One day, he was flirting with a woman he favored in a secluded spot in the imperial garden. Unexpectedly, a priest, a confessor, came by. Because of his wisdom and experience, he had the privilege to approach the prince. Barnabo blushed instantly and felt very embarrassed. But he immediately came up with a devious question to ask the priest: "If you had such a woman in your bed, what would you do?" The priest immediately replied, "Of course, I know very well what I should do, but I don't know what I would do." This answer eased the prince's predicament.

A Florentine man was away from home. He didn't return home until the end of the year, and his wife was in labor. So he suspected his wife of infidelity. He went to inquire of an experienced old woman in the neighborhood whether there were any children born after twelve months of pregnancy. The old woman replied, "Of course there are. If your wife saw a donkey on the day she conceived, she would have to carry the baby for twelve months like a donkey." The husband, after hearing this, actually believed it, and thanked the old woman very much for dispelling his doubts and saving his wife from embarrassment. He finally gladly became the father of the child.

In Florence, a young woman was exceptionally foolish. During childbirth, the baby would not come out for a long time. The midwife held a candlestick and examined her. The woman moaned, "Look over there too, because my husband has worked over there a few times."

Returning from the Esperanto Exhibition 248

— Zuo Qi

In a small room in a Western-style building across from the grand and lively Northeastern Refugee Relief Carnival at its opening, there was an atmosphere of peace and tranquility. The table was covered with colorful books. Striking and touching slogans were posted on the walls, and colorful pictures and stamps were hung, all with a foreign flavor. Indeed, they came from foreign lands, from the ends of the earth. A beautiful and melodious language, neither Mandarin, nor English, nor Japanese, nor any national language, continuously entered the ears. Dozens of young people with hopeful faces browsed through various strange books and newspapers. Furthermore, the most noteworthy thing that caught the eye was the five-pointed green star badge.

This was the first Esperanto exhibition held in Shanghai, perhaps in China!

Anyone who stepped into this room would feel that it was filled with a sense of world consciousness and a peaceful atmosphere. When that solemn song "La Espero" ("Hope") was played from the gramophone, listeners temporarily forgot the noisy and contentious world and longed for a utopian "One World."

Noteworthy in the venue was a framed mirror hanging on the center wall, filled with charred fragments of paper, with several lines of barely legible words in Esperanto. It turned out that these were souvenirs left to us by the god of war. They tell us that the efforts of our Eoperantisioj over the years, like everything else, have suffered the same fate under the tyranny of the god of war.

The second noteworthy thing was that among the Esperanto books and newspapers displayed at the exhibition, publications from Japan and newly emerging countries after the war, such as the Soviet Union, Poland, and Czechoslovakia, accounted for a large proportion, while Esperanto publications in our own country were as rare as phoenix feathers. This may be one of the motivations for holding this exhibition.

Anyone who attends and browses through the various books and newspapers will always see the activity of the overseas labor movement. Looking back at the country, one can only sigh. It is hoped that comrades engaged in the world movement can devote some effort to activities in this area in the future.

Four Great Writers Send Congratulatory Telegrams to Gorky 249

— Yi Xian

The greatest Soviet writer, Gorky, began his literary career in 1892, and this year marks the 40th anniversary. In order to commend his great contribution to the revolution, the Soviet government held a grand celebration on September 25 of this year. Many famous writers from various countries sent congratulatory telegrams. The following are selected translations of congratulatory telegrams from four great writers, including Shaw,

George Bernard Shaw

There are few writers whose works transcend national borders, but Gorky is one of them. In the pre-revolutionary nineteenth century, the first Russian writers to move the hearts of Englishmen were Turgenev and Tolstoy, followed by Dostoevsky, and finally Gorky and Chekhov. Among these, only Gorky made revolution seem possible.

Other writers produced confusing impressions of society, the state, and people, that society was fundamentally terrible, those people were either more luxurious than Peter the Great and the courtiers of the Second Bian Saling era, or (as in Chekhov's novels and plays) were more boring than any characters one could encounter in English and American works similar to the Cherry Orchard. They seemed completely incapable of creating a revolution that ought to be more advanced than America, and more civilized than Berlin, Paris, or London.

Gorky's depiction of Russia is indeed not excessive. He understood the bottom layer of Russia better than other writers (who can all be regarded as gentlemen writers). Although that depiction is darker, as a proletarian literary work, its authenticity has a quality that is lacking in the novels of gentleman writers, whose only ability is to romanticize the surrounding phenomena.

Despair disappeared because of him. The Russian proletariat described by Gorky is filthy, alcoholic, brutal, and ignorant, just like the poorest people everywhere; however, they are also practical in their own affairs. They are not bored, they have the power to grasp "life" tightly, and there is not a trace of the disheartening boredom that gentleman writers take from their boring experiences and write into everything.

In short, because they have revolution in their midst, Gorky's book is a book of dawn, not a book of doomsday. I have only appreciated Gorky's works from translations, and I have only known Gorky himself from two short but very cordial meetings. I think that's all I can say about him.

Romain Rolland

I send my heartfelt congratulations to Maxim Gorky. I wish him many more years of actively guiding the proletarian thought of the Soviet Union and the world.

John Galsworthy

I am very happy to have the opportunity to express my admiration for the great writer Maxim Gorky. I can't help but be happy to think that there is such a name among human beings, and that his complete works have also been published in several countries.

Upton Sinclair

Build a country like this, a country where all the workers are like Gorky - congratulations to him, congratulations to your country.

"Is that someone calling from outside?"

"No. The young mistress made it herself. She said you like to eat this noodle the most."

He couldn't help but ask the nanny at this moment.

"What exactly does that Japanese guy do?"

"He just drinks every day, and after drinking, he dozes off. Sometimes he's not polite at all, and he leans against the young mistress's bed and falls asleep."

Every day, no matter morning or afternoon, I have to go to the church to check the Chinese letters sent from various places for that old foreigner, and write replies for him if they need to be answered. ...A tough job, a tough job!"

Cao Shiguang said, and smiled bitterly for a while.

"Isn't that good? You have extra income."

"It's just this amount."
