Business is Booming 251

— Wu

Once the season arrives, the winter sale is lively again for a long time. The banners of "Big Clearance Sale" and "Buy One Get One Free" are flying cheerfully in the center of the road. Fashionable men and women, with spring breeze on their faces, carry out packages one by one from the department stores, get into cars, and drive away. Everything is booming, everything is a peaceful scene. Moreover, what groups and what groups have now disappeared, which shows that what is being sold is all genuine old-fashioned domestic products, which can further prove that the patriotism of the big bosses is indeed not lagging behind others. Therefore, China is truly promising.

However, there is also such news in the newspaper. In order to believe that I am not dizzy, I respectfully and carefully transcribe it as follows:

"Since October, the import of Japanese goods has been the most crowded. Recently, it was heard that China and Russia have resumed diplomatic relations, and Russian goods will be sold well in China. In recent days, they have been rushing to ship to Shanghai. Yesterday, the Asamaru ship imported more than 18,600 pieces of inferior goods, mainly including textiles, machinery, yarn factory supplies, porcelain, and sugar, which increased the deadweight by one-third compared to when it arrived. On the 19th, 20th, 24th, 27th, and 30th of this month, there are still five large batches of inferior goods, about 60,000 to 70,000 pieces, on the Mikasumaru, Tsukubamaru, Rokkomaru, and Mayamaru, which are rushing to Shanghai by the end of this month.

Of course, this is very interesting news, especially when compared with the current lively market. Moreover, it can be seen that the purchasing power of the Chinese people has long been more than enough. Not only is the domestic product not enough for application, but also the inferior goods have a tendency to exceed supply. Therefore, I suspect that there is no war in Shanghai, and there is no such thing as "national crisis" in China. On the contrary, the word "national crisis" has such a good phenomenon, so the "national crisis" is the more the better, it may as well be a national crisis every year, until the whole of China is a "big sale" and a "big sacrifice."

Finally, I want to say: "Hum! Business is booming, China is really saved."

Science

Electric Clock 252

— Yi

To unify the time in various places, and to have many clocks show the same time, isn't this problem very difficult to solve? Although everyone is using spring clocks, its speed is often either fast or slow, so in the past, major cities in our country fired cannons at noon every day as a signal, which is called the noon cannon, so that the residents of the whole city could adjust their time accurately. However, after a while, each clock often has some differences, so to solve this problem, it is necessary to install an electric clock!

The structure of the electric clock. The electric clock uses the current to rotate the clock hands. Its main parts are roughly electromagnet and gears. Its structure is roughly that there are gears in the center, a hook below the gears, and an electromagnet above the gears. Near one end of the magnet is a soft iron piece, which is connected to the hook. When the electromagnet attracts the soft iron piece, the hook moves and the gear rotates with it. When the iron piece returns to its original position, the gear is hooked by the hook and does not move. The shaft of the gear is also equipped with several gears and other gears, rubbing against each other. The rotation speed of the initial gear and the rotation speed of the final gear are consistent with the rotation speed of the second hand, minute hand, and hour hand of the clock. Therefore, its speed has no differences and delays. Every thirty seconds, the electromagnet can be energized once, then each gear should rotate accordingly. The hour hand, minute hand, and second hand are installed on the axis of each gear, so it can indicate the time like a spring clock. This is the general situation of constructing an electric clock.

The use of electric clocks. Because the time of electric clocks is consistent, it can enable us to abide by the time and not break appointments with friends. Therefore, electric clocks should be installed in schools, parks, palaces, hospitals, factories, major stores, major hotels, and other public places, and at intersections, so that the residents of the whole city can always know the unified and accurate time.

Mother 253

— Yiyi

"Dad! Where's Mom?" Six-year-old Min has been asking her father this way for the past few days. But her father's answer is always just one sentence, "She's gone out."

Mother sometimes goes out, but at most she comes back in two or three days. Why hasn't Mom come back after so many days? This question cannot be resolved in Min's little mind.

Although Min is only a six-year-old girl, she is very well-behaved. She feels that her mother hasn't come home for several days, there must be a reason. Because she saw a tragic scene of tears when her mother didn't leave, although a six-year-old child can't understand it, Min also feels that this is not happy.

"Mom is gone, yes, she's gone. But why hasn't she come back for so long?" Min often opens her big eyes and asks her dad, but her dad's answer is always "She's gone out."

One evening, she saw Dad taking many things to someone to take away. How come the clothes in the box were also taken away?

"Dad! Who are these things for?" Min asked curiously.

"For Mom!" her dad replied. There was also an unhappy look on Dad's face.

"Ah! For Mom! Why do you want to give it to Mom? When will Mom come back?" Min asked her dad again.

"I divorced your mother!" The father unintentionally spit out this sentence.

Min really doesn't understand the word divorce. She asked her father again, "What? When will Mom come back?"

"Mom won't come back!" her father replied.

Ah! Mom won't come back! Why? Min already knew that this time Mom's departure was a bit special. But she still doesn't quite understand that Mom won't come back. At the same time, in her little brain, she remembered a tragic scene when Mom didn't leave, Mom talked to Dad, Dad was very angry, and eventually beat Mom, Mom shed tears, and she also cried, but she cried and cried, was hugged away by the nanny to sleep, and tomorrow she didn't see Mom.

"Mom won't come back! Ah! I want Mom! I want Mom!" Min shouted.

"Child! What are you shouting! What does it matter if Mom doesn't come back?" her father scolded her.

"No! I must have Mom! I must go find Mom!" Min still shouted. And she cried again.

Clerk Correspondence

How to Avenge Shame? How to Prevent It? 254

Mr. Editor:

I have something I cannot understand myself; moreover, I have been greatly stimulated by this matter, and many thoughts have arisen. Now, I will write down the process of this matter below, earnestly asking for your guidance and instruction. The matter is as follows: A certain teacher from ×× University sent his servant to our shop yesterday afternoon to buy a bottle of laxative pills. In the evening, the servant came and said: "After opening the bottle, it was already broken! The pills have changed color, please exchange it for a new bottle." Whether it is the original item, I cannot confirm; I think a respectable teacher would not switch the contents. Because the manager was not present, there was no one to take responsibility, and I am just a powerless employee, how could I agree! The servant who came to speak was quite unreasonable, so I had no choice but to go with him to Mr. So-and-so's apartment. My original intention was to plead earnestly and wait for the manager to return before discussing it. Who knew that after I explained my purpose, (I can frankly say that I had no offensive words at the time). Mr. So-and-so did not show any reaction, but another teacher in the room, seeing that I was small and could be bullied, said very briskly, as if angry but not really angry: "If you don't exchange it, I will hit you, do you believe it!" Before he finished speaking, he raised his fist and sent it towards my face. Fortunately, I dodged quickly and was not injured. Surrounded by oppressive forces, embracing the principle of "a wise man does not fight when the odds are against him," I had no choice but to retreat.

Now, what I do not understand is:

㈠ Can an educated university teacher act so barbarically? Does this matter harm the reputation of the education community?

㈡ How can I avenge my shame regarding this matter? (If I file a lawsuit, I was alone at the scene, with no one to testify, and no injuries, so I will inevitably lose.)

㈢ If I appeal to the school authorities, will I receive a satisfactory response?

㈣ Why are teachers humble towards students but tyrannical towards others? What is their psychology?

㈤ How should I prevent similar incidents from happening again in the future?

Regarding the above five points: I beg you not to give a simple answer like "Great shame | National shame | is already like this, small shame should be endured even more." Thank you! Thank you!

Yu Rui from ×× Shop, opposite ×× University

One. Can an educated university teacher act so barbarically? This is certainly not something that should happen. However, we should also know that so-called black sheep exist everywhere. Among university teachers, there are indeed many who are well-studied and deeply knowledgeable. However, there are also many who, relying on advantageous opportunities, received higher education, even studying in the West, and then became university teachers after returning to the country, but whose actual knowledge is not particularly outstanding. We should not involve others just because one or two individuals behave barbarically. As for the question of whether this kind of behavior harms the reputation of the education community, we believe that the lack of unity and discipline in China's education community today is a phenomenon similar to various problems in the entire country. Everyone is too busy taking care of themselves, so what reputation is there to speak of? Such a "barbaric" act towards you can be considered a very minor matter among the things that harm the reputation of the education community.

Two. Speaking of resorting to legal measures, the editor feels that, as you said in your letter, "Since there is no witness and no injury," it is unnecessary to take such action. If you consider this matter a shame, I think that if you can use this stimulus to diligently engage in moral cultivation, academic research, and conscientious work to promote your career to an early success; when you succeed, this small shame will be completely avenged. You probably don't agree with this answer; but there are two points I want you to pay attention to: (A) A true man should take the responsibility of avenging national grievances as his own, what is a small personal grievance? (B) One of the biggest flaws of the Chinese nation is the excessive separation between individuals and the extremely weak will to fight for public causes. We hope that you will think in the long term and on a larger scale, and take on the responsibility of correcting this trend.

Three. If you talk about appealing to the school authorities, most of the current university authorities are important people and celebrities. They are so busy that they don't even have time to approve official documents, so where would they have the energy to deal with these irrelevant trivial matters? I hope you will not appeal this matter to the school authorities, because appealing to the authorities will not only fail to get a satisfactory response, but may also suffer greater humiliation.

Four. Regarding the teacher's attitude towards students and others, it is generally based on economics, to put it bluntly: it is a matter of livelihood. Because there are students, there is a livelihood; if you are not humble, your livelihood may be in danger. As for "why be tyrannical towards others?" It is just that those below their eye level are prone to encounter this misfortune. Towards those above them, they are too busy flattering! How dare they be tyrannical? This reason is very obvious: for there has never been a person who is arrogant to their inferiors and does not flatter their superiors. If we go a little deeper, although knowledge and morality are closely related, they are ultimately two different things. A person with high morals may not necessarily have profound knowledge; similarly, a scholar's morality may not necessarily surpass everything. (This point is related to Mr. Yu's first question.) We should not assume that university teachers have high morals just because they are intellectuals. Our view of morality should not be determined by form. For example: when we meet kind and hardworking old farmers in the fields, we will naturally feel an unspeakable respect at once; while in the city, we feel that the gorgeously dressed and extravagant merchants are despicable. These two diametrically opposed psychologies are entirely produced by the social environment and the power of morality; therefore, the level of morality is not determined by the level of knowledge. Like Mr. Yu, although in terms of knowledge, you may not be as good as the so-called university teachers, but you still know that hitting someone is impolite, so we undoubtedly acknowledge that your morality is above that of the university teacher.

Five. It is difficult to define a preventive measure for this type of matter. In the future, when dealing with the world, it is best to use the nature of the matter as the standard and deal with the situation at any time and in any place, and of course there will be no difficulty. For example: we believe that your response to the matter you encountered this time was very appropriate. Because the manager was not in the store, you naturally could not exchange a bottle for him at that time. This is very correct in terms of duty. And you immediately went to Mr. So-and-so's apartment with the servant to explain the situation, which can also be regarded as a appropriate way. As for the danger of your face being punched by another teacher, your retreat at the time, although it was surrender, in reality, your personality was unharmed, and the other party's morality was greatly damaged. If you report the situation to the manager after the incident, the manager should be responsible for the negotiation; if he does not negotiate, that is his responsibility. But you stand in a correct position. In short, we should give considerable tolerance to this kind of unreasonable tyranny within the scope of not losing our responsibility and not losing our personality. This is called: "Bearing humiliation and bearing heavy responsibilities," this is called: "A scholar can be humiliated, but cannot be subdued." We hope that Mr. Yu will understand and comprehend from this point of meaning.

Editor's note: This letter could have been kept private, but we believe that there are many shop assistants who are younger, have limited knowledge, and most of them are away from their families and lack close guardians to guide them. They often regard very small stimuli as strange shame and great humiliation, leading to unfortunate incidents. As yesterday's news on the third page of this newspaper reported: Wu Panzhang, an apprentice from Anhui Province at the Universal Hat Factory on Yokohama Road, Zhabei, who is seventeen years old, committed suicide by smoking opium after arguing with a colleague. This is an example right before our eyes. This situation is not a blessing to society and makes us feel very uneasy. Therefore, we have answered Mr. Yu's letter point by point, hoping that dear apprentices, whenever you encounter unreasonable tyranny, do not be overly impulsive and do many unexpected things. This is one of the purposes of this open letter.

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (12th Installment) 256

— Qin Shouou

"That's right! You were a famous clever devil in those days! You guessed this matter of mine!" She was simply as clever as I am. "However, I didn't plan to hide it from you; and I very much intend to discuss it with you. Because you know: he completely deceived me, and I am now determined to negotiate with him!"

Her later reversal greatly exceeded what I could have imagined.

"For this kind of dispute between men and women, you must hire a lawyer to negotiate. ... But, aren't you also a full-fledged Bachelor of Laws?" To be honest: I myself can't think of a satisfactory solution to my dispute with you, so I took the last resort of fleeing. How can I plan for her! Therefore, I replied with humorous and irrelevant words.

"I'm talking to you seriously, don't mess around! Hiring a lawyer is very much in line with my own plan! Isn't Zhou Dajing a lawyer in Shanghai?" I really admire the forgetfulness of our Empress Dowager. She said the name of her old lover, Zhou Dajing, who used to be with her all day long, and spent money on her like a young master, as if he was an ordinary old classmate, without any hesitation.

"That's right! He has quite a reputation in Shanghai. You are old classmates. If you go to him, he will definitely not rip you off!"

She picked up the glass and took a sip of tea, smiling leisurely.

"You, ... have you seen him recently?" I planned to use a step-by-step offensive strategy to bring up the old stories between her and Dajing, and scold her thoroughly.

"No." She was still smiling, as calm as if she had never said half a word to Zhou Dajing before.

"He still misses you very much! He misses you very badly!" I took another step forward.

"Didn't he get married a long time ago!" She began to resist.

"But, he doesn't love his wife; he still loves you!" I boldly threw a hand grenade.

"Haha! ... Haha! ... Haha! ..." The result of throwing this hand grenade was that she couldn't help but put down the teacup, looked at me with a contemptuous look, and laughed wildly.

"Haha! ... Haha! ..." One minute, two minutes, ... she continued to laugh. She laughed so hard that her whole body was shaking. I still haven't understood why she was laughing, and I was always stunned. Several gentlemen on the side who were trying to doze off were also awakened by her crazy laughter, and looked at me and her with surprised and questioning eyes.

"Haha! ... Haha! ..." She was laughing without regard for her life, and I was laughed at so much that I didn't know what to do.

"Hey! Hey! Miss Li! Can you stop laughing for a while?" I had to retreat from the offensive position to the position of surrendering.

"Haha! ... Haha! ..." It was hard to end her laughter. She laughed so hard that tears came out.

"What was so funny about those two sentences just now that you laughed so hard?" I quickly asked her the reason for laughing.

"Haha! ... Haha! ..." She almost laughed again. But, she tried her best to hold back her laughter and said two shocking words very frankly, "Dajing doesn't love his wife, but you love his wife."

Rare News in the Film World

Is Suzanne Bianchetti a Comedian? (Part 2) 257

— Furen

More than ten years ago, the West Cecil B. DeMille or Lubitsch was an Eric von Stroheim of German origin. One day, Stroheim was alone in his office and slammed the table, flying into a rage. He said, "Why can't I find a suitable woman for my film? I don't have a single good person under me, they are all useless!"

Stroheim looked up and saw a thin and weak woman standing in front of him.

"What's your name?"

"My name is Suzanne Bianchetti."

"What a joke! What kind of name is that? Why would a good person have such a terrible name?"

"You're right, sir. These are the names of my two aunts, and my name is in memory of them."

Stroheim smiled and said quickly, "It doesn't matter, it doesn't matter, we can try it first."

The film that Suzanne Bianchetti was acting in at that time was called "Greed". Bianchetti played a greedy and ruthless woman. Stroheim went all out and shot more than a hundred reels (over ten million feet). Later, he cut it into an eight-hour film. This film probably hasn't been released publicly. It was indeed a failure, but it was an economic failure, not a technical failure. Now all the big films that pass through are the incarnation of "Greed" and cannot break away from the artistic mold of Stroheim.

At that time, only six people had seen the test screening of "Greed". They are now scattered in all directions and can still remember the greatness of this film. They all expressed infinite respect when they mentioned Suzanne Bianchetti. Stroheim repeatedly exclaimed during the test screening, "Suzanne Bianchetti is the greatest tragedian of her generation!"

But the roles of tragedians are very few, and even the greatest tragedian of her generation has to eat. Her eyes are very interesting, and the movements of her hands can make people laugh, so after many trials and tribulations, she had to change her career. Playing only tragic roles would lead to starvation.

It is true that "environment changes temperament, nurture changes the body." Suzanne Bianchetti changed into comedic roles, and her stiff demeanor gradually faded. Her views on everything in the world have also changed. She is now one of the most outspoken women in the world. Not only can she make people laugh, but she often makes fun of herself to find happiness.

Recently, she had a story. When filming "All Quiet on the Western Front," director Carl Laemmle remembered Suzanne Bianchetti's appearance in the film "Greed," so he invited Bianchetti to play the role of the poor German woman. When the film was finished and ready for the test screening, everyone laughed when they saw Suzanne Bianchetti. This was not a funny film, but as soon as Suzanne Bianchetti's face appeared, the audience would laugh without waiting to see her performance. Therefore, that part of "All Quiet on the Western Front" was later reshot with a different person.

Suzanne Bianchetti's tragic era has passed, flowing eastward like water and cannot return. Stroheim, old and with failing eyesight, watched her perform one comedy after another, making people laugh. He still clenched his fists, bitterly cursing the reversal of the world and the demise of genius. (End)

Charles Farrell once won first place in the All-American Beautiful Man election in 1927. His golden age has not completely passed even now. Although he ranked fourth this year, he has consistently been number one among male stars for five years. "Seventh Heaven" was the beginning of his good luck in his life and the goal that people will never forget and admire. In the sound world, his masterpieces include "Four Devils," "Tear Stains," "Butterfly Drunk with Flowers," and the recent "First Year of Marriage." Of course, Janet Gaynor is his old partner.

Domestic News

Two Inventors of Sound Film Machines 258

— Ming

China's first sound film was "After the Rain Clears", which was produced in Japan. After the September 18th Incident, Huaguang Company could no longer stay in the eastern neighbor, and its own capital was insufficient, so it announced its closure.

Then came the mighty Tianyi, which was originally a small company. Unexpectedly, after the studio caught fire, the Shaw brothers made a big decision, hired seven technicians, and bought a complete set of "Western Electric" machinery. They successfully produced ten sound films in a year. Recently, it is said that they have abandoned foreign employees such as "Xu Guo" altogether, but the machine is foreign-made and still cannot be considered purely domestic.

The Startone of the Mingxing Company first used wax discs to record "Singer Red Peony," which was quite successful, so they also bought a set of American radios, but how can that be considered domestic?

The only Chinese sound films we have seen are these. Originally, we didn't even have silent film cameras or film in our country, so why should we demand sound film cameras? However, facts are beyond people's expectations. Some people have invented domestic sound film cameras.

The first person to research this sound machine was Yan Heming. He spent five years of hard work and actually succeeded. Of course, it is not a 100% invention. Most of it can be considered imitation, but to take a step back, being able to imitate successfully, or even surpass the original, is already a supreme glory for China, a country with backward industry. He named it "Yan Su Tong". The first film was produced by Hengsheng Company, "Spring Tide" started filming for half a year and is about to be published. The results of the filming are said to have the momentum to surpass imported films.

The second is Mr. Zhu Qingxian. He and Mr. Yan can be considered the great heroes of the Chinese film industry. The machine he made is called "Qingxian-style Sound Film Machine."

When Wang Fuqing heard that he had succeeded, he ran to sign a contract to shoot a "Spring Breeze and Willow" film. Later, Mr. Zhu also made a "Winning Glory for the Country" for Fudan Company. These few days, the location shots have been completed in Hangzhou.

Don't ask how the performances are, how the sound is, for the above three films, because they are purely Chinese-made sound films. However, it is expected that they will not be bad. In any case, the two Yans and Zhus have indeed contributed to the Chinese film industry.

Translation of Famous Works

The Face on the Screen (Middle) 259

— Translated by Dun Ruo

"I guess your life isn't very comfortable, is it?" Philip asked her. At first, she didn't answer, but later she said:

"If my husband didn't have a mental illness, everything would be fine. When he has an episode, even four men can't hold him down on the bed. Usually, he just sleeps in a daze. When he was hired by Boss and Chebes, a piece of iron fell on his head. Of course, the doctor said that the illness wasn't caused by the piece of iron, but because he drank too much alcohol. Maybe the doctor is right. Not long ago, I fell on the street. The doctor said I was malnourished. Alas, after taking the seventy fenni advance, I still have to pay rent and gas. What else can I use?" She said in a hoarse and monotonous voice.

"Well, then go see Mr. Chepeki. He may be able to help with your life," Philip encouraged her. So he unconsciously got off the train without knowing which station he had stopped at. Triga Arski shook his head gently after he left.

The following is the beginning of her amazing film career.

She walked into the elegantly decorated Harvard office to see Leonard Chepeki. Chepeki looked at her with great hope. She stood in the middle of the room, not understanding what was going on, but she wasn't panicked. She felt indifferent to everything. From then on, she worked here, and she could earn ten marks a day. She couldn't believe her luck.

There were already many women here who were dressed as raggedly as she was. Their faces were also painted with wrinkles and shadows like hers. She was pushed back and forth by them, but she never felt that she was also a part of this crowd. In this crowd of painted masks, her truth was terribly real. A kind of indifferent expression flowed out naturally from her heart. Her eyes were strongly stimulated by the arc lights, and tears kept flowing down. At one o'clock, all the actors went to the dining hall to eat, but she didn't go with them. She sat in a hidden corner of the studio and took out a piece of bread from her oilcloth bag and ate it. Chepeki almost bumped into her.

Work started again at half past eight in the evening. Philip stood on a large ladder in front of her. Behind them, many people used megaphones to order them to move forward. They had instructed Triga Arski that if she heard the slogan "Go now," she had to leave the crowd and go to the stairs. She walked very naturally. She left the crowd and shielded her eyes from the bright lights. Her tears were flowing so badly that she couldn't see anything. The photographer on the wooden frame excitedly turned his crank like crazy.

"Unbelievable, unbelievable," someone whispered. "Come again tomorrow. We want to shoot a solo performance," Chepeki said to her later. She filmed for three consecutive days and earned thirty marks.

Random Talk

Discussion on Film Title Translations 260

— Jianan

The name of a film encompasses the essence of the entire script. Before seeing the entire film, the audience has a considerable concept of the content after reading the title. Therefore, it will determine whether to watch it or not. Therefore, the title is directly related to the box office appeal. In today's cinemas, regardless of the content of imported films, they are always translated into names that are sensual, erotic, and cater to the general social psychology. As a result, audiences often feel disappointed and curse. But sometimes there are very good films that suffer a tragic fate of a deserted theater because the translation is bland. Indeed, for the endless stream of films produced, it is really difficult to use titles that are not repeated and must be novel and unique. However, for business reasons, cinemas must pay attention to the following principles when translating titles:

(1) Faithful It is necessary to use novel names for advertising, but the translation must be fully consistent with the story. The truth cannot escape the audience's eyes, and deception can only happen once. There will eventually be a day of failure if you desperately use ×× Erotic History and ×× Spectacle to attract audiences.

(2) Popular and Elegant A name with poetic meaning is certainly very elegant, but for the general audience who don't understand it well, a profound classic is too uncommon.

(3) Avoid Direct Translation When Possible Because of the differences in customs and human feelings between the East and the West, it is not necessarily suitable to translate their commonly used words into the national language. As for uncommon specialized terms, using transliteration is even more undesirable.

(4) The Translations Must Be Consistent This is a specific instruction for theaters that show second-run films. Using different translations for films that have already been shown, and not posting the original name, often makes audiences unwilling to watch again.

Film Anecdotes

Gong Qiuxia's "Little Lover" 261

— Xingxiu

Recently, many female stars have entered the film industry from the song and dance world, such as Wang Renmei and Li Lili, who have already enjoyed considerable fame. The film industry's attention to talents in the song and dance world was caused by these two. Gong Qiuxia of the Meihua Song and Dance Troupe also has news of entering the film industry, but because the conditions cannot be agreed upon, she cannot fulfill her wish early. In the previous issues of this journal, Qingxia and Yinguang both made mistakes in their short history of her. Before joining the Meihua Song and Dance Troupe, she did join the Putao Song and Dance Troupe. Wu Peixian was also a member of Putao, and they met at this time. She and Wu Peixian co-starred in "Little Lover," with Wu playing the male role. Both of their performances were innocent and lovely, and they are still praised today. Unfortunately, Wu died early. Wu was indeed a woman. The mistake of thinking she was a man may be because she played a male role in "Little Lover."

Film Treatise

From Tears to Laughter 262

— Chen Dabei

Now, please try the eighth expression self-study method in front of the mirror again.

Your breathing can help you wrinkle your brows and the corners of your eyes to resemble a crying face, and tears will naturally flow out. Take a closer look, are there any parts of your face that resemble a smile? Of course, there won't be. The corners of the lips turn upward when smiling, and downward when crying. This is obvious, isn't it? But that's not enough. With a slight carelessness, your lips might open slightly, and when captured by the camera, the result still resembles a smile. Many famous stars have clearly cried real tears, but the result is similar to a smile, simply because their lips were not tightly closed.

Therefore, I am specifically calling your attention here. When you go to the studio for practical training in the future, when you are performing a crying scene, do not neglect your lips.

The ninth expression self-study method is going from tears to laughter.

Continue to use the method of slowly inhaling and exhaling through the nostrils while silently counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" to gradually make a crying face. Maintain this crying face, while silently counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" in your mind. While slowly exhaling, the muscles of your face gradually relax, transforming from a slight smile into hearty laughter. At the same time, you should carefully observe in the mirror what kind of changes have occurred in the muscles around your eyes and the muscles above and below your lips.

Today's Highlights

### Two Comedians Courageously Advocate for Righteousness 263

Comedian Doctor Han Lingen and comedian master Yi Fangshuo, deeply concerned that their voluntary participation in various performances might be affected by prior engagements in outside performances, potentially causing timing issues, have both volunteered to each host a performance. Whenever there are gaps in the performance schedule, the two gentlemen will use their own comedic talent to entertain enthusiastic guests. The two gentlemen's spirit of courageous advocacy for righteousness is truly admirable. Enthusiastic guests who hear this will surely welcome it unanimously.

### Cha Ruilong's Car Passing Over Body 264

Martial arts movie star Cha Ruilong has long been known as a strongman in martial arts circles. This time, he is performing daily with famous Shanghai martial artists to promote martial arts and showcase their unique skills. This is truly an unparalleled opportunity for those concerned about martial arts. Tonight, he will perform the car passing over body stunt. Please pay attention.

### Group Harmony Lion Dance Cantonese Opera Performance 265

The Qunhe General Association's Sanyu Society is famous throughout Shanghai for its lion dance. This time, they are participating in our association, presenting their unique skills daily, enough to invigorate drooping spirits. Famous Cantonese opera singers are known throughout Shanghai for their singing. This time, motivated by patriotism, they are taking turns coming to the association to sing voluntarily. Those who love to listen to Cantonese opera can both hear famous performances and help the Northeast, achieving two goals with one action. Don't miss the opportunity.

### The Entire Venue Is Decorated With Startling Impact 266

This time, the venue decoration focuses on propaganda. Everything that enters the eye and ear aims to inspire alertness. For example, the Nenjiang Bridge battle scene by the Northeast Miniature Painting Academy, the remnants of the Zhabei battlefield of the current war, the "Outcries from Outside the Pass" painting by the Fine Arts Academy, and the fragmented rivers and mountains on the Northeast map are all enough to shock people's minds and encourage patriotism. The purpose of the performances is to invite people to pay respects to fellow countrymen suffering under national crisis. Please everyone come to pay respects and cry together.
